British House of Lords Debate on China Policy: Lord Peel Advocates Strengthening Britain's Position in China, Emphasizing the Development of the Chinese Market for Imperial Trade, and Assisting China with Constables to Restore Order in the Yangtze River 41

(London) In the House of Lords today, former Secretary of State for India, Lord Peel, during a debate on British policy towards China, praised the inherent commercial realism of the Chinese and their diligence in business even in adversity. He continued by saying that while Britain should indeed develop trade with Russia, it should pay particular attention to the Chinese market because the Chinese people are more numerous and China is more amenable to trade concessions. British policy towards China is always important, but especially so today, given the changing world situation and the difficulties facing British trade.

Revising the Attitude Towards China: He wondered whether the government, in light of this new environment, had also considered revising its attitude towards China. The current government's policy towards China has an excessive tendency to drift with events. If the Chinese believe that we are merely observing, then we cannot hope to gain their respect. Other countries are not relaxing in the slightest and are constantly eager to consolidate their position in China.

Against Financial Assistance to China: Lord Peel then spoke of the success of the Nanjing government and T.V. Soong, saying that Soong had resigned from the war, but he felt that Soong would soon reappear. Britain has known China longer than any other Western country. History proves that Britain has no aggressive or territorial ambitions. Britain's policy in India has proven that Britain does not seek any dominant interest in China. Britain can assist China with constables, so that order can be gradually restored in the Yangtze River basin. If order in the Yangtze is not restored, then none of the Nanjing government's plans will be able to bear fruit. He did not advocate providing financial assistance to China.

The Issue of the British Envoy's Residence: Lord Peel then spoke of the issue of the British envoy's residence in China, saying that while he did not suggest that the British envoy should reside in Shanghai, he felt that many difficulties had arisen because there was insufficient contact between the British envoy and the British community in Shanghai. As for the issue of re-assigning the ambassador, he felt that Britain should send an ambassador to a country in the Far East as important as China.

Maintaining Troops Stationed in Shanghai: Lord Peel concluded by speaking about the Shanghai issue, citing the Feetham Report, especially the section on the independence of judges, saying that this is an international issue that requires the cooperation of the powers. He also said that the withdrawal of British troops stationed in Shanghai occurred at the same time as the construction of large Japanese barracks in Shanghai. He felt that the current moment is the most opportune time to re-define policy towards China.

Supporting Peel's Proposals: Sir Holroyd, a director of Imperial Chemical Industries, supported Lord Peel's remarks and spoke of the company's director, McGowan's, travels in China, hoping that other British industrialists would do the same. Lords Lugard and Eddington then spoke in succession. Eddington was the Custodian of Enemy Property in China from 1923 to 1928. He advocated that the embassy should not be located in Peiping and expressed regret over the reduction of British troops stationed in Shanghai.

Lord Stanhope Speaks: Lord Stanhope spoke, saying that Sun Yat-sen had invited him to participate in one of China's revolutions. Regarding trade with China, he welcomed McGowan's visit to China. The British government holds a sincere and friendly policy towards China. Britain's goal is to maintain good relations with organized governments. Britain is willing to accommodate the national aspirations of the Chinese people to the greatest extent and recognizes the powerful national sentiment throughout the country.

Constable Assistance 42

Should be Proposed by China: Therefore, he felt that the first step in Lord Peel's suggestion that Britain could assist China with constables should come from the Chinese side. If China does make such a suggestion, then the British government will certainly be willing to consider to the best of its ability what kind of assistance can be given to China.

Relocation of the Embassy 43

Not Necessary at Present: As for the issue of relocating the embassy, it has been considered for a long time, but the government does not believe that relocation is necessary. It is still questionable whether relocation can increase the efficiency of the embassy. Furthermore, sanitation and expenses should also be taken into account. The Chinese government has moved its capital once or twice. If the British embassy moves to Nanjing, there is a risk that this move would be futile. Furthermore, from a health perspective, Peiping is better than Ningbo and Shanghai, and Shanghai is particularly objectionable. Shanghai has its own special difficulties, and it is feared that the British envoy stationed in Shanghai will divert his energy. As for Lord Lugard's proposal to continue allocating funds from the Boxer Indemnity Fund for the expenses of the University of Hong Kong, the British government has no right to handle it.

Actions Towards China 44

Strive to Avoid the Suspicion of Interference: In summary, the difficulties of China continuing to move forward are ones that the Chinese people can solve on their own. In this regard, the British government has taken more actions than other countries to express its friendship and sympathy for reasonable wishes. It is not easy to see what Britain can do without involving the suspicion of interfering in China's affairs. (Reuters, 8th)

Embassy Moving South 45

The Government Considers it Inadvisable: (London) The government representative replied to Lord Peel in the House of Lords yesterday, stating that the British government considers it inadvisable to move the British embassy in Peiping to Nanjing, but the issue of whether the British envoy should reside in Shanghai or Ningbo will not end as a result. The Archbishop of Canterbury wrote to The Times today, saying that with the cooperation of the Chinese people, the British can accomplish much, as evidenced by the establishment of customs and postal services, and Simpson's dredging project in the Yangtze River basin. However, it is questionable whether the British in Nanjing can move the Chinese as the Americans have. If the British envoy resides in Nanjing himself and is not six hundred miles away from the administrative center, then the situation may be different. The British envoy's departure from Peiping for Nanjing is truly abandoning the most beautiful city and moving to a new capital under construction, but this move by the British envoy can at least be dutiful to Britain. Many people with relations to China have long advised the government to establish a residence for the British envoy in Ningbo or Shanghai, and other countries' envoys to China spend most of their time in Shanghai, which Britain can emulate. It is generally believed that Parliament will propose this matter again soon. (Reuters, 9th)

King of Afghanistan Assassinated: Crown Prince Ascends the Throne at Only Seventeen Years Old, British Government Greatly Concerned Upon Hearing the News, British Troops in Northwest India on High Alert 46

Kabul: King Nadir Khan of Afghanistan was assassinated at three o'clock yesterday afternoon in the palace by a trusted courtier. His son, Zahir Shah, succeeded him to the throne. The new monarch is only seventeen years old and is expected to be assisted by his uncle and Prime Minister, Hashim Khan. After the sudden incident, the authorities immediately cut off transportation and imposed strict security, while investigating the inside story of this act, including whether there was a conspiracy to assassinate the entire royal family and whether the army had any disloyal intentions. Regarding the assassination of the king, only the announcement that King Nadir Khan had been assassinated by a traitorous minister has been issued, while other details remain secret, as there is a strong suspicion that there is a political assassination group attempting to assassinate the royal family, such as the assassination of the brother of former King Amanullah, Aschas Khan, by a twenty-seven-year-old student at the Berlin embassy on June 6 of this year. At the same time, the king's nephew, Adak Khan, was also seriously injured, and it is feared that there may be some clues related to this assassination case. Therefore, the Afghan authorities are currently conducting a strict investigation in Berlin and domestically, because since the deposed King Amanullah visited Berlin in 1928, the city has become the most intensely contested place for various factions in Afghanistan. According to reports, the late King Nadir Khan was Amanullah's nephew. In 1929, after Amanullah was driven out by the rebel Habibullah, the government troops finally recovered the capital, killed Habibullah, and enthroned Nadir Khan. The city of Kabul is as peaceful as usual. Upon hearing that the new monarch had ascended the throne, the people flocked to the vicinity of the palace to pay their respects and celebrate, expressing their loyalty. (National Telegram, 9th)

New Delhi: The British Embassy in Kabul has verified the news of the assassination of King Nadir of Afghanistan and said that the assassin was a student, probably one of the Afghan students previously expelled from Germany. There are concerns that the barbarians on the British border may take the opportunity to pour into Kabul to plunder, but the Afghan army has sufficient funds and good discipline and may be able to support the new monarch. According to a Bombay dispatch, the entire country of Afghanistan is now in mourning for Nadir and has unanimously announced its allegiance to the new king. (Reuters, 9th)

(London) The British Emperor sent a telegram to the new King of Afghanistan today to express his condolences. A Rome dispatch states that former Afghan King Amanullah, upon hearing the news of Nadir's assassination, stated that he was not involved in any disturbance. Afghanistan does not yet have sufficient education to accept new policies, so he does not wish to return to the throne. According to general opinion in Rome, if the people of the country unanimously wish him to return, then Amanullah can return to his homeland. He is very happy residing in Rome, and his young children have almost forgotten Kabul, while his eldest son is currently working as a lawyer in Rome. (Reuters, 9th)

(London) This morning, the British government received an official telegram stating that the assassin of the King of Afghanistan was a student, not a courtier. (National Telegram, 9th)

(London) The British government is greatly concerned upon hearing the news of the assassination of the King of Afghanistan. Officials in the India Office remained on duty all night, closely monitoring the development of events, fearing that all Islamic regions would be affected and new disturbances would occur in the area near the border between India and Afghanistan. British troops stationed in northwest India are on high alert. Here, the news of the King's assassination was first received by the Afghan embassy. (National Telegram, 9th)

(London) The Afghan Ambassador to Britain took a flight from here to Paris this morning to discuss the current situation with the Ambassador to France, and then to the Afghan capital, Kabul. The Afghan Ambassador to France is the brother of the assassinated King Nadir. According to a Reuters dispatch from New Delhi, the circumstances of King Nadir's assassination are still in question. Even the Indian Foreign Ministry has not received news of the King's assassination, relying only on Reuters' news for information. Nadir's assassination is likely the result of infighting between supporters of Nadir and those plotting the restoration of former King Amanullah. Nadir had a brother killed in Berlin, and political assassinations have repeatedly occurred in Kabul last year, all due to infighting between the two factions. Nadir was fifty-three years old this year. In 1929, King Amanullah abdicated and power fell into the hands of Habibullah. Nadir led troops to resist and won a great victory. On October 16 of that year, he ascended the throne. Amanullah was previously abandoned by the people for vigorously implementing new policies and reforming old customs, but some places still admired him, and after several years, the past was gradually forgotten by the people. Therefore, Amanullah was unwilling to remain an exile for long and was said to have intended to return to his homeland. Kabul's Acting Foreign Minister told a Reuters reporter that the authorities had been concerned about the occurrence of events for some time. The opinions of various parties in Afghanistan are deeply divided, and it is difficult to predict what will happen next. When the king was assassinated, the prime minister and foreign minister were not in the capital. The prime minister is loyal and is Nadir's half-brother, so he should be loyal to Nadir's son. The crown prince is twenty-one years old and has his father's style. (Reuters, 9th)

The Second Higher Civil Service Examination: Civil Law Questions from Yesterday's Test 58

(Nanjing) The second Higher Civil Service Examination began on the morning of the 9th. The roll was called at 7:00 AM in front of the Examination Yuan, with a total of 602 people present. Five people were absent due to reasons. The exam began at 8:00 AM. All categories included Civil Law questions for judicial officials, with three questions: (1) "Termination of contract, revocation, withdrawal, and dissolution of conditions" are similar in nature to resolving a contract. Please describe the differences between them to clarify the nature of dissolving a contract. (2) A, B, C, and D form a partnership, with A and B contributing capital, and C and D contributing labor. Later, the capital is repaid, but the debt is still less than 4,000 yuan. C happens to have a loan to creditor E for 4,000 yuan, and E insists on using this money to offset the debt. If A and B are indeed unable to pay, please describe the legal relationship between each person. (3) The difference between a husband and wife's inherent property and original property. After the property is divided, who should the remaining property belong to? There were also three questions for ordinary administrative and other categories: (1) What are the powers of the administrative agency in charge of the purpose and activities of a legal person according to the Civil Code regarding legal persons? Please elaborate. (2) Do married but underage men and women have the capacity to act? Can they independently enter into a contract for a marital property system and divorce without the consent of a proxy? (3) A rents a house from B, agreeing to hand over the house on November 1st. When the deadline arrives, B does not hand over the house, and A stays in a hotel. That night, a fire breaks out in the hotel, and A's luggage is burned. Is it reasonable for A to demand compensation from B for the burned luggage and the hotel expenses? Please discuss. (Central News Agency, 9th)

(Nanjing) Secretary-General of the Examination Yuan, Xu Gongwu, stated that a total of 838 people were admitted in the screening tests in Peiping and Tianjin. Although the average scores of the rejected papers were failing, many had particularly excellent scores in one subject. A reward system is planned. Those who score 80 points or higher in the rejected papers of both the screening and regular tests will be given prizes. (Central News Agency, 9th)

In case of unexpected changes, what will the future hold? This is the third reason. In short, the arrival of Sun's troops has a hundred disadvantages and no advantages. Chairman Lin Enjoys Scenery in Fujian, Does Not Discuss State Affairs, Leisurely Attitude, Worships Ancestors, Sweeps Tombs, and Plays with Antiques 95

Fuzhou Correspondence: Chairman Lin Sen of the National Government returned to Fujian on the Yingrui warship from Nanjing on the 23rd of last month. It has been over half a month, and he spends his days touring mountains and rivers, not discussing state affairs. He has a very leisurely attitude. From the 24th to the 26th, he stayed at the residence of his clansmen in Chengpu Tou, Fuzhou, and visited Cangqianshan, Gaigai Mountain, Hongshan Bridge, and the West Park. On the 27th, he returned to Shanggan Township to worship ancestors, Fenggang Township to sweep tombs, and Lujia Township to inspect elementary schools. On the 29th, he went from Shanggan Township to Qingzhi Temple (under the jurisdiction of Lianjiang County) for sightseeing. On November 2nd, he went from Qingzhi Temple to Fulu Temple (under the jurisdiction of Fuqing County) for sightseeing. He only returned to Fuzhou on the 8th. He is now awaiting a meeting with Chiang Kai-shek before accompanying Navy Vice Minister Li Shijia on the Yingrui warship to Sanduao to inspect the naval port, and then he will return to Nanjing. Lin's entourage was very simple during this trip. Except for staying at the private residence of his clansmen in Fuzhou and lodging at the Qingzhi and Fulu temples, he stayed in the Hai Ping steamship prepared by the Mawei Naval Port Headquarters. As for banquets, except for attending a public banquet given by his clan in the ancestral hall of Shanggan Township, he declined all other banquets. However, he would caress and examine antiques presented by antique dealers, and he would inquire about old friends in detail. If they were poor, he would give them money, but if they asked him for a job, he would decline, citing financial difficulties and personnel congestion. (November 8th)

Guo Rudong's Troops Destroy Bandit Nests on the Hubei-Jiangxi Border, Destroyed the Pseudo Northern Route Headquarters 96

Nanchang Communication: The counties of Xiushui, Wuning, Tonggu, and Ruichang in northern Jiangxi, which border the counties of Chongyang, Tongshan, and Yangxin in eastern Hubei, have the Mufu Mountains, which are the watershed between the two provinces. The terrain is treacherous, the atmosphere is closed, and Peng Dehuai established a bandit's nest here in 1927. After Peng's bandits fled south to the border area of Jiangxi, Hunan, and Guangdong, Kong Hechong occupied it again, using Longgang Yanxia Youju Paibu Jiugongshan Pao Mountain and Lieyao Mountain as their nests. They established various pseudo-organizations, and their poison spread to dozens of counties on the borders of the three provinces. Last year, Chairman Chiang himself supervised the suppression of the Red bandits in the three provinces of southern and eastern Hubei, and the bandit nests were successively recovered. However, Kong's bandit nests were still not completely cleared due to the complex terrain. The communist leader Zhang Tao took the opportunity to summon and reorganize the remnants of southern Hubei and set up a pseudo Northern Route Army Headquarters in Dawu Mountain, where Wuning and Xinyang meet, to command the bandits in southern Hubei. They echoed each other with Kong Hechong's pseudo Sixth Army Group on the border of Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan, and with the bandits on the border of eastern Hubei, Henan, and Anhui. After He Jian moved into Pingxiang, he ordered the 123rd Corps to advance toward Li Tianzhu, Kong Hechong, Cai Huiwen, and Zhang Tao. Guo Rudong of the Third Corps moved into the Yanxia bandit area and coordinated with Yue Sen and Tao Guang of northern Jiangxi, and Chen Guangzhong and Li Jue of eastern Hunan to besiege the bandits. They also paid attention to reconnaissance of the bandits' tracks in order to attack them unexpectedly. On October 21, Guo's troops ambushed at Gaojia Mountain and captured Zheng Xianglin, the company commander of the special task force of the pseudo Northern Route Headquarters, and seized letters written by the bandit leaders, learning that the pseudo Northern Route Headquarters and the Southeast Soviet Government were both gathered here. Therefore, he divided his troops into five routes, secretly and rigorously searching Dawu Mountain, Dongkeng, Meikeng, and other places, and destroyed the bandit's central organs. Yesterday, the Corps Commander Chen Jicheng telegraphed Chiang to report the victory. The original telegram stated, "According to Division Commander Guo Rudong's telegram, according to the captured bandit company commander Zheng Xianglin, an intercepted letter from bandit Chief of Staff Deng Gongheng to bandit Northern Route Commander Zhang Tao revealed that the bandit's general organ was near Mount Yaolie. I immediately dispatched parts of the 151st and 152nd Regiments and the engineer battalion in five routes to search Dawu Mountain, Dongkeng, Meikeng, and other places in Wuning, destroying the bandit's Northern Route Headquarters, General Hospital, military clothing factory, supplementary battalion, and cadre training team, killing over 200 bandits, capturing over 70 bandits, including Zhang Nianyou, political commissar of the bandit's 9th Regiment, and Cheng Chongyan, political commissar of the bandit's 7th Regiment, rescued hundreds of refugees, seized seven guns, three telephones, one load of Western medicine, a "bundle" of a 1:100,000 scale map published by the bandit's red printing bureau, and various important documents. The remaining bandits fled into the deep mountains." After Chiang received the telegram, he issued an order to commend them, saying, "This division's success in destroying the bandit nests is due to prior preparation, planned reconnaissance, and swift and secret use of troops, which enabled them to achieve great results. In addition to issuing an order to commend them in order to highlight their achievements, it is hoped that the subordinate units will be informed."

The Headquarters received a telegram from Songpu from Peng Zhenshan, commander of the 30th Division, reporting to Chiang on the progress of advancing to suppress the Red bandits on the border of eastern Hubei, Anhui, and Henan, stating, "Following Commander Sun's (Lian Zhong) order to suppress the bandits in the west, the bandit nests in Gengyang Zhenshan, Daxiaojunshan, Ziyangshan, and Yaojiazhai have been broken, and many pseudo-organs and bandit repair shops have been destroyed. The remaining bandits fled in two groups, one group of over a thousand people fled to Laojun Mountain, where they were intercepted by the 13th Division, and the other group of several hundred people fled to Tuanbanhe Qijiasakan. I led parts of the 30th and 31st Divisions to pursue and eliminate the bandits from Macheng to the north." He was also ordered to be commended. (7th)

Under the Oppression of the Communist Bandits, the Tragic State of the People in the Bandit Areas, Economic Panic, Forced Issuance of Public Bonds, Using Large Meetings to Coerce People into Joining the Bandit Army 97

Nanchang Communication: Since the Communist bandits have been surrounded and blockaded by the National Army, internal panic has become increasingly serious. The latest situation of the bandit side is recorded as follows:

Regarding the economy: 1. Attempt to sell 3 million in public bonds, 2. Vigorously carry out land investigation movements and report on the locations of rich peasants, 3. Actively promote thrift movements, taking all food savings to help the war effort, 4. Use lectures to promote the sale of public bonds. At the meetings, all personnel from organizations and groups should enthusiastically speak, and deductions should be made for public bonds from food savings. Regarding military affairs: 1. Each county and district should try its best to expand the bandit army, with all Red Guards joining the bandit army, 2. The bandit leaders, seeing that forcing people to join is not as effective as deceiving, enticing, and threatening, have implemented the following measures: (1) The trade union announces that if trade union comrades do not attend when concentrated, their land will be confiscated, (2) The Communist Youth League committee should nail a "shameful plaque" on the door of those who do not join the Communist Youth League International Division. The bandit military department should assign them to forced labor teams, (3) The slogan used to deceive workers is "Joining the Workers' Division can get good land", or "If you want to get land, you have to be a bandit soldier", (4) When mobilizing the (model battalion) Red Young Pioneers to join the bandit army, do not do any mobilization work in advance. When it is necessary to concentrate in Ruijin, just say that you are going to Ruijin to attend a meeting, (5) Use two silver dollars and one luo of grain to buy a person to be a bandit soldier, or imitate Huichang by using three to four silver dollars to buy ten people to mobilize, (6) Imitate Changting's method of mobilizing model regiments to join the bandit army, deceiving them to cooperate with the Eastern Army to fight the 19th Route Army, opening to Hetian, and then explaining that they are joining the Workers' Division, 3. Launching the Workers' Division has caused a serious phenomenon of the Workers Division and the Communist Youth League International Division scrambling for soldiers, 4. Those who do not become bandit soldiers will have their property sealed, 5. Designate how many bandit soldiers to expand, 6. Copy the names of the masses aged 16 to 45, and the district Soviet will immediately send people to this village (to give the "glory plaque"), and designate the concentration by name, 7. Use the opportunity of opening a mass meeting to close the front and back doors, and ask them to register as combatants. Regarding the prevention of desertion: 1. Try to provide food so that there are no parts of the country where they only eat one meal of porridge a day (which shows the suffering of the bandit side), 2. Report the reactionaries and strictly prevent those who are forced to desert in batches (which shows that most of the bandits want to surrender).

Regarding political work: 1. Organs and political commissars should guide the organization of "shouting" on the front line, and suitable personnel are required, such as enemy soldiers, many from Hunan, so more Hunan people are sent to be responsible for shouting, 2. It is strictly forbidden to scold stray soldiers, 3. The bandit side is extremely panicked by internal shaking and has shouted the following slogans: "The enemy has built so many fortresses, how long will it take to finish fighting", "The enemy has more planes and also releases poison gas, we have no way to deal with it" (it is noted that the National Army does not use poison gas, and small leaflets have been made by the political training office of the headquarters and distributed by plane, so that the people in the bandit area will not be deceived by the bandits), "Our strength in southern Jiangxi is too thin, and the main bandit army does not come, so there is no way to win", "After the fourth encirclement and suppression was broken, there was a fifth, and in the future there will be a sixth, seventh, and eighth encirclement and suppression, and I don't know when it will end."

The attitude of the people in the bandit areas towards the bandits: 1. In Huichang Xunwu Anyuan, several divisions have expanded the bandit army into a group of terror, 2. Every time a mass meeting is convened, no masses come because they are afraid of becoming bandits, 3. The people in some places have organized broadsword associations to confront or disturb a certain area of the bandits. (November 7, Datong Society)

Ping Sui Railway: Debt Dispute - Railway Bureau Cancels Interest for Creditors, Creditor Group Holds Meeting to Discuss Debt Recovery 98

Beiping Correspondence: The Ping Sui Railway was built with employee investments. Now, the railway bureau, under the pretext of streamlining debt, has cancelled interest payments for creditors holding 1,000 yuan in debt, proposing to repay the principal in 100 months, with monthly installments of 10 yuan and cessation of interest. Accrued interest will not be paid. Consequently, employees have organized the Ping Sui Railway Bureau Short-Term Loan Creditor Group to demand debt repayment from the railway bureau. Today (the 4th), an emergency meeting was convened at 4:00 PM, deciding to first send representatives to petition the authorities and to contact various parties for assistance. Regarding the details of the loan, Creditor Group members Yang Weiru and Wu Zhenchen stated that China and Russia began trading very early, with the trade occurring at Boketu, north of Kulun, commonly called the "Trading City." The trade route ran from Beijing, exiting Juyongguan, passing through Zhangjiakou, and entering Inner and Outer Mongolia to reach Kulun. This was formerly the only land trade route. In particular, the Juyongguan pass, which cuts through the Taihang Mountains, is known worldwide as a natural fortress. This road is exceptionally important for national defense and commerce, thus attracting the attention of major powers. During the late Qing Dynasty, in the Guangxu era, when foreign powers were most aggressively invading China, they each divided China's hinterland into spheres of influence. The Russians designated the area from Beijing to the north, specifying that if China were to build a railway along this route in the future, it must use Russian loans and be constructed by the Russians. They urged its early construction, threatening to plan it on our behalf if we delayed. China, in order to maintain its sovereignty, reluctantly decided to build it itself. At that time, the patriotic engineer from Guangdong, Zhan Tianyou, was appointed as the chief engineer. Coincidentally, the Jing Feng Railway was experiencing prosperous business, with annual surplus remaining after repaying British loan principal and interest. This surplus was allocated to the Jing Zhang Railway as construction funds. From then on, the plan for the Jing Zhang Railway to be built purely with Chinese people and Chinese funds was set. The Jing Zhang Railway officially commenced construction in the 31st year of Guangxu and was completed in the 34th year. Construction costs were entirely allocated from the Jing Feng Railway surplus. After completion, in the first year of Xuantong, it was proposed to extend the line to Suiyuan, named the Zhang Sui Extension. Construction costs continued to be allocated from the Jing Feng surplus. By the autumn of the 3rd year of Xuantong, only the engineering train reached Yanggao County in Shanxi. The Wuchang Uprising occurred, causing major political changes, and the project was halted. At the same time, the construction funds for this line also ran aground due to various other factors. At that time, the section of the extension project from Tianzhen to Yanggao was still largely incomplete. From Yanggao to Datong, there were only a few sections of earthen road. In the 1st and 2nd years of the Republic, the political situation stabilized slightly, and plans were made to complete the Datong section first. Because funds were unavailable and it was inconvenient to borrow foreign capital, the railway staff devised a method to maintain the railway. The bureau director and chief engineer initiated the issuance of short-term loan bonds of 1,000 yuan and 10,000 yuan each, with a term of one year or one and a half years, a monthly interest rate of 7.5%, interest paid quarterly, and principal repaid upon maturity. Staff were encouraged to subscribe with their salary savings, raising 300,000 to 400,000 yuan to maintain the railway project. This fundraising served as the underlying fund for the project, while the operating revenue of the Jing Zhang section was used for revolving capital. The Ministry of Communications provided a guarantee for the repayment of principal and interest on this loan, and the purpose of the loan was listed on the back of the loan bond to ensure transparency. This was the general situation regarding the initiation of short-term loan bonds at that time. After the Datong section opened to traffic in the 3rd year of the Republic, the line was extended to the Tongfeng section. In the 5th year of the Republic, the Datong Kouquan branch line was built. In the 7th year of the Republic, the line was extended to the Fengsu section. In the 9th year of the Republic, the line was extended to the Ping Sui section. In the 11th year of the Republic, the line was extended to the Sui Bao section, gradually completing the entire Jing Sui Railway, reaching Baotou, totaling more than 1,600 li. This was largely thanks to the annual revolving fundraising of these short-term loan bonds. After the 5th and 6th years of the Republic, this method of borrowing gradually gained credibility, and subscribers included not only railway staff but also many people outside the railway. The total amount borrowed also gradually increased. Between the 10th and 11th years of the Republic, the railway bureau purchased too many locomotives and vehicles, and new project expenditures were also significant. Due to the political situation, the central government's finances were tight, and for other various reasons, the railway bureau's situation deteriorated daily, with finances in dire straits. Loans were obtained from banks at a monthly interest rate of 1.7% to 1.8%, requiring the designation of revenue from various stations as collateral, along with other various conditions, before they could be established. At that time, many of these short-term loan bonds had matured and needed to be repaid, but the railway bureau was not only unable to repay them but also believed that this method of borrowing had benefited the railway bureau for a long time. There were no kickbacks, no collateral, and it was purely a direct credit relationship with depositors. As long as credit was maintained and payments were handled properly, it was much cheaper than relying on the whims of bankers. Therefore, the railway bureau automatically changed the interest rate to 1.5% and converted the matured loan bonds into extended loan bonds. Later, when the extended term expired, it was changed to being able to be withdrawn at any time. The railway bureau's repeated automatic changes to the method were all to alleviate the distress of depositors due to its own economic deficiencies and to avoid the embarrassment of withdrawals, as well as to leave room for maneuver for the future. (4th, Jin)

Highways in Southern Anhui Counties, Huainan-Wuhu Railway Also Planned for Construction 99

Wuhu Correspondence: The highways in this province, as stipulated by the Seven-Province Highway Conference for the construction of trunk and branch lines, are all under active design, aiming to complete construction within the second deadline at the end of this year. In southern Anhui, in addition to the Xiuxian-Shexian line, which has long been completed and open to traffic, the Huizhou-Hangzhou Road will also be completed within the month. The Jingdezhen-Qimen-Tunxi-Chun'an and Wuhu-Tunxi-Wuyuan-Dexing lines are either raising funds for construction or are already under survey and construction. Because they are related to transportation in seven provinces, a summary is presented as follows:

Jing Qimen Line 100

Qimen borders Chunliang in Jiangxi, serving as an important route for travel between Jiangxi and Anhui. Mail from Jingdezhen is transferred through Qimen to various places, as Qimen is connected to various counties in southern Anhui. Therefore, the Qimen-Jingdezhen line holds the throat of land transportation between Anhui and Jiangxi. The Anhui Construction Department previously approved a letter from the Jiangxi Highway Department urging the dispatch of personnel to conduct a detailed survey of the road in order to discuss and decide. Now, the Anhui Highway Bureau has commissioned engineer Xu Chuanjing to conduct a survey to Chunliang, and to discuss the method of starting construction with the Jiangxi side in Jingdezhen.

Wuhu Tunxi Road 101

The earthwork on the Jixi section, which is the most difficult part of the road to construct, has recently been completed by 80%. However, the stone bridges and culverts still need additional labor to rush construction. The northern section starts from Wuhu. From Dawang Village to Wuhu, there is no roadbed. The Construction Department has ordered the Highway Bureau to remeasure a new line and carry out filling and construction as soon as possible. Preparations are also being made to expand the site at the junction with the Huizhou-Hangzhou Road for the use of vehicle transfer. The originally planned traffic route for this road will be changed because the construction of the Jingjian Road (Capital to Jianping) project is under active construction, and the route will be extended through Jixi to Tunxi. The route from Beijing to Anhui can be transferred from the Jingwu Road to the Jingjian Road to Tunxi. It is expected to be completed and open to traffic by the end of this year.

Tunxi Chun'an Line 102

Starting from Tunxi and reaching Chun'an in Zhejiang, it is connected to the Wuhu-Tunxi Road, serving as an important route for transportation between Anhui and Zhejiang. In order to complete the highway plan, the Anhui Construction Department commissioned Ding Maiman as the chief engineer to survey the road. Recently, he led a team to survey and complete the project. The total construction cost is estimated to be more than 500,000 yuan. As the road is related to transportation between Anhui and Zhejiang, active fundraising is underway to start construction as soon as possible.

Wuyuan Dexing Line 103

This route runs from the county seat of Wuyuan to the Baisha Pass in Dexing, Jiangxi, where it connects to the Huabu-Dangshan highway, serving as an important route for Wuyuan and the counties under Raozhou to enter Shanghai and Hangzhou. Initially, the county had planned to repair it itself, but it was abandoned due to insufficient fundraising. Recently, the Huining Association of Wuyuan, which is based in Shanghai, repeatedly telegraphed the Anhui Provincial Government to build a motor road due to the obstructed transportation in Wuyuan. The Construction Department believes that this road is very important for commerce and that there is a need for repair. It should be listed as a county road, with the local government raising funds and attracting merchants to build it. Orders have been given to the county government to engage in fundraising. When this road is completed, the transportation of goods between Raozhou and Wuyuan will all enter and exit through this road, which is more convenient than shipping through Poyang Lake, Xunyang, and Tunxi.

The Central Construction Committee recently has a plan to lay a light railway from Luhezhen in Huainan, this province, to Wuhu. Chief Technician Chen Maojie and Technician Shi Weixin were dispatched to Wuhu to survey the area around Chaohu last month. It is also heard that the light railway from Luhezhen to Hefei can be built by the end of this year. The reason is that Huainan in this province has extremely rich coal reserves. According to expert statistics, there are more than 240 million tons, enough for a century of mining. However, transportation from the mining area (Luhezhen in northern Anhui) to Wuhu is inconvenient, and even if mining is possible, transportation is not easy. Therefore, the Construction Committee has a proposal to lay a railway. (5th)

National People's Electricity Association Representatives Arrive in Hunan - Hunan University Hosts Banquet 104

Changsha Correspondence: After the fifth annual meeting of the National People's Electricity Association concluded on the 5th, the Changsha Electric Light Company of Hunan specially welcomed the representatives and invited them to visit. The association elected more than 20 representatives. That evening, they departed on the special express train to Hunan-Hubei, arriving in Changsha at 8:00 AM on the 6th. They first went to the Xianghan Hotel for rest. In the afternoon, they visited the north and south power plants, accompanied by engineers Yang Botao and Yi Dingxin, and were quite satisfied. They then toured Tianxin Pavilion for photography, and accompanied by the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, visited the Hunan Orphanage National Products Exhibition Hall in Juicaigarden. In the evening, the Hunan Power Plant hosted a banquet for the representatives at the Guan Yue Temple, and invited Director of Construction Department Yu Jiechuan, Changsha Mayor He Wenyuan, and Public Security Bureau Chief Li Qiong to accompany them. During the banquet, Xiao Enzhen, chairman of the company, delivered a welcome speech. Chairman Li was elected by the representatives to give a reply. After the banquet, they went to the Xiang Theater to watch a play.

On the morning of the 7th, the representatives crossed the Xiang River to visit the scenic spots of Yuelu Mountain, paid homage to the tombs of revolutionary martyrs Huang Kecheng and Cai Songpo. At noon, Hunan University hosted a banquet, and President Hu Shuhua delivered a welcome speech, saying that he was honored to have the guests travel far to visit. The gathering today is different from ordinary events because many graduates of the Electrical Engineering Department of the College of Engineering of the university are serving in the electric plants of the guests. The future graduates still need the guidance of the guests to meet the environment of both sides and promote the benefit of both parties. Therefore, the relationship between the association and the school can be said to be extremely close. The steel industry is the key to saving the country. He is preparing to submit a preliminary plan for the Zhuzhou Steel Plant to the government. Both steel and electricity are pioneers in developing the industry, and there is a possibility of cooperation between them. He asked the guests to point out the problems in his books. The university's location is the original site of Yuelu Academy. The sages who studied hard and became talents here were replaced by people of generations. The students can still abide by the ancient training, study hard, and the school style is simple. This can be said to be gratifying to the guests. Please take a glass, wishing the Electricity Association a long life and the guests a healthy journey. Then Li Yan gave a reply, saying that the university's excellent style is known to colleagues, and President Hu is an engineering expert. The students' grades should be very good. The association is focusing on concentrating talents in view of the importance of the engineering departments of the members, and hopes that the Electrical Engineering Department will create practical talents to meet the needs of the electricity industry. In the future, it is hoped that the education sector and the electricity industry will cooperate with each other for the benefit of both parties. Then the guests visited the library which was completed on the previous day. Hunan Power Plant only had to cancel the planned tour of Hengshan because the representatives had to return to Wuhan on the evening of the day. At 4:00 PM, a farewell banquet was held at Wanlichun Western Restaurant. The guests and hosts gave speeches during the banquet. After the banquet, the representatives boarded the train and returned to Wuhan. The representatives will give speeches at Wuhan University on the 9th and visit the scenic spots of Luojia Mountain, and then they will return to their respective homes. (8th)

Wuxi

Octogenarian Marries Ninth Wife 109

Feng Heqing, who runs a carpentry shop in Daxu Lane in the Fourth District, is already 80 years old. His beard and hair are like silk, but he is mentally and physically strong, showing no signs of aging. He has married seven wives in his lifetime, and his eighth wife also passed away in August of this year. Feng, feeling lonely in his old age and unaccustomed to being a widower, recently married a widow surnamed Wang from the northern mountains as his successor, through the mediation of his relative Gu. The marriage was officially consummated on the 6th of this month. For a time, people near and far were talking about it.

Mediation Fails in Huisheng Debt Case 110

Xi Huian, the owner of the Huisheng Silk Factory in Huigong Bridge, fled to Shanghai after owing more than 60,000 yuan. The County Chamber of Commerce is handling the liquidation on his behalf and is in contact with Magistrate Yan. First, 952 dan of dry cocoons piled up in various warehouses of the factory were sealed by official Ji Songzhen, accompanied by Fan Xinzhi, the director of the Second Branch Bureau, on the 7th of this month. It is learned that yesterday afternoon (8th) at 2:00 PM, the Chamber of Commerce invited more than 60 representatives from relevant banks, money houses, silk cocoon warehouses, and individual dry cocoon households to discuss the settlement of the individual dry cocoon household portion. Qian Sunqing served as the temporary chairman, reporting on the process of mediating the debts of the Huisheng Silk Factory. Next, representatives of the individual dry cocoon households demanded the payment of more than 35,000 yuan and requested that bankers lend cash to be distributed equally. However, representatives of the bankers refused to lend money because the dry cocoons had been mortgaged by Xi Huian for approximately 80,000 yuan. After deducting interest, warehouse rent, insurance, and other expenses, there was little left. After a long discussion, the two sides insisted on their own opinions, resulting in no way to resolve the issue. Finally, at the request of Chairman Qian, the bankers offered 30% cash to compensate the individual dry cocoon households. The bankers only agreed to 25%, totaling more than 9,600 yuan, to be distributed first. The representatives of the individual dry cocoon households found the amount too far apart and difficult to cope with the villagers, so the matter remained unresolved. In recent days, villagers have been sitting and demanding payment from the individual dry cocoon households, with as many as 30 or 40 people at each house. As a result, disputes have arisen repeatedly. The wife of the owner of the Changchang Cocoon Firm in Zhanggaozhuang in the 16th District, surnamed Mou, was driven to desperation and committed suicide by hanging herself the day before yesterday. Fortunately, she was discovered and saved, and no fatal case occurred. Furthermore, silk cocoon merchant Wu Shirong fraudulently received more than 100 dan of dry cocoons of the Xi family from the Yixin Cocoon Warehouse. This was discovered by the individual dry cocoon households, which led to another negotiation.

Rugao

Dispute over Farmland Leads to Murder 116

Wang Lian, a carpenter of Suye ethnicity in Daijiagang, Dongzhuang, Baibu District, Rugao, was honest and kind. The day before yesterday, a dispute arose with his cousins Wang Dashan and Wang Xishan over farmland. It began as a verbal argument and then escalated into a fight. Wang Dashan and others beat Wang Lian to death. Afterwards, Wang Dashan and others threw Wang Lian's body into the river in an attempt to cover up the crime. However, the body suddenly floated up. Witness Wang Liu ran to report to the Lin Branch Precinct. The township head, Shen Zhonglu, also reported to the District Office. The District Office, because the case involved human life, immediately reported to the county government, requesting that personnel be dispatched for inspection. Magistrate Lin, upon receiving the report, personally led an inspection official, secretary, and others to rush to the scene for inspection.

Jiaxing

Suspicion of Manslaughter by Second District Militia 117

On the night of the 24th of last month, the militia of the Second District of Jiaxing, led by squad leader Lin Fanhou, along with militiamen Pan Yongxiang, Zhu Yishun, Li Mengyu, Shen Dalin, and township head Mei Jiaren, were patrolling. A Shaoxing boat sped by. They ordered the boat to stop for inspection, but the boat did not respond. Suspecting it was a bandit boat, they strenuously pursued it and fired two shots, inadvertently hitting Huang Weijin in a vital area. He fell into the river and died instantly. The next day, the deceased's son, Huang Zikun, went to the river where the incident happened to recover the body. The militiamen detained him, took him back to the team, searched his home, deemed Huang Zikun's behavior improper, and sent him to court for interrogation. After the case occurred, Prosecutor Tong Xianzhi believed that the militiamen were suspected of manslaughter. Yesterday, he summoned both parties for interrogation again. As a result, squad leader Lin Fanhou, militiamen Li Mengyu, Pan Yongxiang, and Huang Zikun were all ordered to post bail.

Finance Minister Kong Returns to Shanghai This Morning - Hosts Banquet for Banking Sector This Afternoon 119

All American Wheat to be Transported by China Merchants Bureau - Delegation to American Company, Fraser & Uruguhart - First Batch of American Wheat Starts Shipping to Shanghai 121

Due to the transportation issues, the purchased American wheat resulted in significant disputes. It wasn't until yesterday that they were finally decided. China Merchants Bureau will rent ships to America. However, the American company, Fraser & Uruguhart, is commissioned by China Merchants Bureau, and will handle the rental of ships and the carrying of passengers and goods. A contract has been signed. The following is the history of this matter:

Fraser & Uruguhart Undertakes Cotton and Wheat Loading 122

This time, China has ordered a large batch of American relief cotton and wheat, the amount is very large. All loading will require at least 200 ships. If transported in rotation, it will require at least 200 transports to complete. Last year, the American company, Fraser & Uruguhart, previously represented the Central Government in transporting more than 300,000 tons of relief wheat, charging a very small amount of freight, almost entirely as a volunteer. This year, the cotton and wheat was delivered by this company. As the companies charged excessive freight, only Fraser charged low fees. And because last time the company was helpful with the wheat delivery, the American side allowed the cotton and wheat to be loaded by this company. The contract has been signed. All import procedures have been negotiated. The American cotton has already arrived.

Changes Mid Way 123

Before the American wheat was ready to be loaded, the Central Government disagreed on this matter. The reason is, the American wheat was purchased by the government, therefore the government should be the one transporting and loading. Why was this delegated to a foreign company? China Merchants Bureau is a national shipping company, and therefore can handle this matter. The Fraser contract was already signed, therefore problems resulted. However, Fraser had already contacted several American shipping companies.

The Difficulty of Shipping Goods 124

Although the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (招商局) can take over and charter ships to load wheat, if empty ships go to the United States to transport wheat to Shanghai without loading any goods for the return trip, the shipping costs will be huge and the freight rates will be high, making it more expensive than Fook Lai's (福來) freight rates. Moreover, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company does not have branches in the United States and is unfamiliar with the local conditions, making it difficult to compare with Fook Lai. Therefore, after discussions, the Cotton and Wheat Transportation Office also believes that it cannot entrust the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to be solely responsible for transportation. After a long period of discussion, a compromise was finally reached.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Responsible for Handling 125

As a result of the agreement, all matters related to wheat transportation will be handled by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. However, the procedures for chartering ships and the transportation of export goods from Shanghai, Hong Kong, and Luzon (小呂宋) when the wheat ships arrive in Shanghai, unload their cargo, and return to the United States will be handled by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and Fook Lai jointly. All matters related to the delivery and unloading of goods in the United States will be handled by Fook Lai. In this way, empty ships going to the United States can be avoided, and freight costs can also be reduced. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and Fook Lai have been meeting for several days to discuss this matter, and it was resolved yesterday.

Both Parties Sign a Contract 126

Regarding the joint transportation of American wheat, the contract between China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and Fook Lai has been agreed upon and signed by both parties. Fook Lai will be responsible for chartering ships in the United States to transport wheat. After the ships arrive in Shanghai, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will be responsible for unloading and storing the wheat. Both parties will work together to solicit the transportation of American goods for the return trip. All authority will be vested in the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and Fook Lai will only act as a broker, extracting a minimal commission. After signing this contract, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will send personnel to Fook Lai to discuss wheat transportation and other matters.

The First Shipment is Scheduled 127

The first batch of American wheat was originally scheduled to be loaded onto ships early on, but it was delayed for many days due to the aforementioned issue. Now that this matter has been resolved, the first batch of American wheat can be shipped from Portland, USA, and is expected to arrive in Shanghai in about twenty-three or four days. Therefore, it can be imported at the end of this month or the beginning of next month, and will be completely unloaded at the China Warehouse (華棧) and Yangzi Wharf (揚子碼頭). In the future, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will send ships to transport the wheat to other ports.

The Second and Third Batches of Cotton are Coming 128

The second batch of American cotton, which is being transported by Fook Lai's ships, has been confirmed to have departed from New Orleans and is expected to arrive in Shanghai around December 10th. It will also be stored in the China Warehouse. The third batch of American cotton was shipped about ten days later than the second batch and is expected to arrive in Shanghai on the 22nd or 23rd of next month. According to reliable information obtained by reporters, two batches of American cotton, totaling about 30,000 bales, will arrive in Shanghai every month from next month onwards.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Board of Directors Approved the Water-Land Joint Transportation Contract Yesterday. The Joint Transportation Office Will Prepare a Fair Copy for Official Signing. Preparations for the Longhai Railway Joint Transportation are Completed and Ready to Be Implemented on Schedule. 129

The State-Run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Ministry of Railways' Joint Transportation Office have agreed on a contract for the joint water-land transportation of cargo throughout the country. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's board of directors approved it retroactively yesterday. Preparations for the Longhai Railway joint transportation are completed. The details are as follows:

The Board of Directors Approved the Contract 130

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Joint Transportation Office have agreed on a water-land joint transportation contract. First, Yu Tan (俞棪), the Director of the Joint Transportation Office, and He Quansheng (何泉聲) and Sun Zhenwu (孫振武), the Commissioners of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, signed the contract and brought it to Shanghai. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company held a board of directors meeting at 4 PM yesterday. The attendees included Zhang Shouyong (張壽鏞), Ye Zhuotang (葉琢堂), Du Yuesheng (杜月笙), Wang Xiaolai (王曉籟), Yang Zhixiong (楊志雄), Hu Yunzhuang (胡筠莊), Sheng Pinchen (盛蘋臣), and Liu Hongsheng (劉鴻生), among others. First, Liu Hongsheng, the General Manager, reported on the process of negotiating and finalizing the water-land joint transportation contract with the Joint Transportation Office, as well as the approval by the Standing Committee. He requested retroactive approval. The meeting resolved to grant retroactive approval. Then, they discussed the plan to transport American cotton and wheat to China with Fook Lai. The meeting adjourned at 5 PM. It is said that Liu Hongsheng will sign the contract today and report it to the Joint Transportation Office by telegram. The Joint Transportation Office will then prepare two sets of official contracts for formal signing.

Preparations for the Longhai Railway are Completed 131

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has designated commissioners to be responsible for handling water-land joint transportation and is separately negotiating with various railway bureaus to proceed. It is expected to be fully implemented on December 1st. As for the Longhai Railway joint transportation, it is scheduled to be implemented on the 20th of this month. The temporary warehouse at the Laoyao (老窰) Sunjiashan (孫家山) Station is scheduled to be completed on the 15th of this month. Chen Yongjie (陳永傑), the newly appointed Deputy Director of the Haizhou (海州) branch, has arrived in Laoyao. All preparations are completed. The Tonghua (同華) steamship is scheduled to depart from Shanghai for Haizhou on the 19th and load the first batch of joint transportation cargo for return to Shanghai on the 21st. The Kang Zhengji (康正記) Towing Barge Company has decided to send two barges and five experienced boatmen and staff to Laoyao, Haizhou, immediately to handle the transfer of joint transportation goods.

Zhou Songnian Talks About the Haizhou Joint Transportation 132

A reporter from the Xin Sheng (新聲) News Agency met with Zhou Songnian (周頌年), the Chief of the Traffic Department of the Longhai Railway, at the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company yesterday. According to him, the negotiations have been completed and he will take the Shanghai-Ping (北平) passenger train back to Haizhou tonight (i.e., last night). The temporary warehouse and pier at the Laoyao Sunjiashan Station will cost 80,000 yuan to complete. As for the joint transportation pier, it has been changed to Laoyao because Dapu (大埔) has been silted up in recent years, and a 1,000-ton seagoing vessel can only load 400-500 tons of coal each time and is prone to running aground. As a result, a lot of cargo on the Longhai Railway is stored in the Dapu warehouse. Now, the Laoyao pier can accommodate 3,000-ton seagoing vessels, which is more convenient. As for the Dapu pier, it will not be abandoned because the Longhai Railway handles about 30,000 tons of cargo per month, and Dapu is a center for salt. Therefore, companies such as Da Zhen Hezhong (大振合衆) will not be unable to operate due to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's handling of water-land joint transportation.

Liu Chongjie Will Go Abroad, His Family and Entourage are Scheduled to Go to Europe Next Month, and the German Chamber of Commerce Held a Banquet for Envoy Liu Yesterday Afternoon 133

Liu Chongjie (劉崇傑), the newly appointed Chinese Ambassador to Germany and Austria, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning on the Beijing-Shanghai night train after going to Beijing and Jiangxi to meet with Director Wang and Chairman Jiang. He attended a banquet hosted by the German Chamber of Commerce at noon and will leave Shanghai in a week, taking a detour through Japan and the United States to take up his new post in Europe. The details are as follows:

Liu's Remarks 134

Liu told a reporter yesterday morning that he had gone to Beijing and Jiangxi to meet with Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan, and Chiang Kai-shek, the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, to seek instructions on German diplomatic affairs before coming to Shanghai. He plans to leave Shanghai in a week for Japan, where he will stay for three to five days. He may return to Shanghai or go directly to Europe via the United States. Liu stated that he has no mission in Japan and it is entirely a private trip. He used to work at the embassy in Japan 15 years ago and has not been to Japan for many years, so he is going for a visit. Going to the United States is also a sightseeing trip, with a stay of about ten days before going to Germany to take office. China had a full-time ambassador to Austria ten years ago, but recently it has been concurrently held by the ambassador to Germany. He will first go to Berlin to present his credentials and then to Austria. There will be no changes in the staff of the two embassies. He is only taking a few people with him on this trip, including his secretary Lei Xiaomin (雷孝敏) and his entourage Wang Shijing (王世京). They will take the Italian ship Conte Rosso (康脫羅素輪) from Shanghai directly to Europe on the 12th of next month with his family.

German Chamber of Commerce Banquet 135

At noon yesterday, the German Chamber of Commerce in Shanghai specially hosted a banquet for Ambassador Liu at the German Club at 454 Haig Road (海格路), with German Consul General Bayer and others as guests. Liu went to attend at 11:45 AM and the guests and host enjoyed themselves until 1:30 PM.

French Envoy Wilden, French Consul General Meleia and the commanders of the army and navy went to the dock to greet them. He also said that he is very interested in Far Eastern affairs and will re-examine Japan's industrialization after arriving in Tokyo. Lin Fusheng, a Young Chinese Aviator Studying in Germany, Will Fly Back to China. He Was Sent by the Central Government to Study Military Aviation in Germany. He Once Crashed Near Berlin. He Graduated Last Month and Plans to Follow Sun Tonggang's Heroic Feat. 144

German aviation technology has always been highly respected in the world. The Chinese government has sent personnel to Germany to study aviation, and there are quite a few of them. Since Mr. Sun Tonggang flew back to China from Germany, he has been admired by the people of the country. Now there is also Mr. Lin Fusheng, who has graduated from aviation studies in Germany and plans to follow up with a long-distance flight back to the country. A reporter from the Min Yan (民言) News Agency learned the details from Mr. Lu, a friend of Mr. Lin, in Shanghai yesterday, and is urgently reporting it as follows:

Studying Aviation 145

Mr. Lin Fusheng is a native of Minhou, Fujian, and is 27 years old. In 1929, he graduated from the Central Military and Political School. After being selected and retained for study abroad by the school, he went to Germany to study aviation on May 28, 1930. The school Mr. Lin attended was the German Aviation School, located in Braunschweig (勃郎威克) in Hanover (漢諾堡) near Berlin, the German capital.

Lin Fusheng, a Young Chinese Aviator Studying in Germany 146

Mr. Lin's main subjects of study were various military technologies on land and water, and he also studied aircraft machinery manufacturing. He graduated in three years. Mr. Lin first studied land-based flying in Germany, then water-based flying, and finally combined land and water practice. According to recent observations by German military aviators, land and water aircraft are very important for future coastal defense and air combat. Because of his study of amphibious flight, Mr. Lin often flew between the north and south of Germany, because northern Germany is suitable for water-based flight.

Once in Danger 147

On February 9 last year, Mr. Lin was practicing airplane rotation and ascending and descending in a Dr 499 aircraft near Berlin. The plane crashed and was completely destroyed, but Mr. Lin only injured his jaw and teeth. He was hospitalized for eight weeks, and for seven weeks he only drank and did not eat, but his spirit and physical strength were able to remain as before. At that time, the January 28th Incident (淞滬抗日戰事) broke out, and Japanese aircraft arbitrarily bombed. Mr. Lin was extremely angry and indignant upon hearing the news in the hospital. He wrote to a friend, saying that the minor injury did not kill him, and that he had kept this body to resist Japan and save the country. Mr. Lin's ambition can be seen.

Mr. Lin Once Crashed and Was Rescued 148

About to Return Home 149

Mr. Lin graduated in October of this year. Before graduating, he often flew between the north and south of Germany and various countries in Europe, including Spain, to practice long-distance flying. In order to promote aviation to save the country, Mr. Lin plans to follow Sun Tonggang and purchase an aircraft in the near future to make a long-distance flight from Europe to Asia to return to China. He is currently applying for approval from Chairman Chiang, Zhang Zhizhong, the Dean of Education of the Central Military Academy, and the Training Supervision Department.

The Cotton Cloth Exchange Opened as Usual Yesterday Morning. The Ministry of Industry Sent Liu Fuyin to Shanghai to Mediate. All Parties Have Understood and Resumed Business as Usual. 150

The Chinese Cotton Cloth Exchange was ordered by the Ministry of Industry, at the request of the Cotton Industry Control Association, to refuse customers to hand over newly produced yarn from November to the end of December, causing a three-day disruption. Zhou Bingwen, the Standing Committee Member of the Cotton Industry Control Association, and Mu Ouchu, the Chairman of the Exchange, went to Beijing to discuss everything with the Ministry of Industry. The Ministry of Industry immediately sent Liu Fuyin, the Director of the Department of Agriculture, and Zhou to Shanghai to mediate. The day before yesterday afternoon, they convened a meeting of important figures from yarn manufacturers and Mu Ouchu, the Chairman of the Exchange. After careful discussion by both parties, the result was very satisfactory, and the Exchange convened a temporary board of directors meeting at 4 PM on the same afternoon. At the same time, the Brokers Association also convened an emergency meeting in the afternoon to report everything. They separately obtained the consent of the members and decided to open as usual yesterday. A disturbance has come to an end. A reporter from the Xin Xin (新新) News Agency went to the Exchange yesterday morning and learned that the cotton yarn market has recovered. However, the external clearance of the alternative method, that is, the so-called exchange of new yarn for old yarn, is still not fully understood. The reporter inquired with the Brokers Association, which stated that the so-called alternative method, such as refusing to accept new yarn delivered by customers in accordance with the order of the Ministry of Industry when cotton yarn is auctioned, and then having the Cotton Industry Control Association exchange this new yarn for stored yarn, is probably not as simple as that. It is best to hope that the Ministry of Industry can withdraw its order and develop a proper method to take into account the interests of both parties.

Large-Scale Dumping of Foreign Matches, Our Match Industry Is on the Verge of Extinction. Our Country Will Levy Dumping Taxes on Foreign Matches. The Ministry of Industry Plans to Grant Monopoly Rights to National Matches. 157

In recent years, foreign matches have been dumping goods in China at depreciated prices, becoming more and more serious. As a result, national matches have been excluded and are in danger of collapse. A reporter from the Ri Ri (日日) News Agency specially visited the person in charge of the Ministry of Finance's Shanghai office yesterday and asked for countermeasures. It is said that this matter is not a local issue, but the entire issue of our country's industrial sector. It is necessary to plan from the root cause and solve the problem fundamentally. It is not beneficial to the country and the people to try to save only one type of match. As for the temporary solution, it should be handled by the Foreign Goods Dumping Review Committee, which will determine the collection of match dumping taxes based on the facts. In addition, according to an official from the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry has long been aware of the dumping of foreign matches and has drafted a national match monopoly, which is the government's initial step to save national matches. It must be decided by the central government whether the monopoly issue is feasible. The current relief method is to levy a match dumping tax, which is enough to counter the dumping.

Two Railways Reported the Method of Fire Alarm Signals 158

Regarding the fire incidents on the two railways, the resident police station submitted a proposal to the bureau affairs meeting that when a fire is encountered, the locomotive should sound its whistle with specific signals to help report the fire. The resident police station has now agreed with the locomotive department to stipulate that continuous whistling of the whistle with two long sounds and two short sounds will be the signal to report a fire. The locomotive sections have been instructed to comply and the police sections have been informed.

Joint Transportation Begins, The Speed of Freight Trains, The Maximum Speed on the Two Railways, 35 Kilometers Per Hour 159

The plenary committee of the Capital Ferry Traffic Preparation Committee and the representatives of the railways decided on the issue of the speed of freight trains. The railways informed each other that the maximum speed of freight trains on the two railways is 35 kilometers per hour. The locomotive department informed the Tianjin-Pukou Railway locomotive department, and they replied that the current method of adjusting the tonnage and load is based on the speed of 12 kilometers per hour when the freight car is on the highest slope and curve, which is the minimum speed, and the maximum speed is "approximately 35 kilometers." The locomotive department has also transferred this to the traffic department for review and reference.

New Development in the Future of China's Cooperative Construction; General Office Established in Shanghai; Office Established in Wuxi 165

In the past, the national cooperative business was handled by the government authorities, and a cooperative association was established to specialize in guiding the cooperative organization. However, no private individuals invested in the national cooperative construction movement. For several years, due to the lack of relevant cooperative knowledge among the people, the results often tended to be unsuccessful. Although the authorities tried their best to find ways to hire experts to study, the key was that theory could not be effective. Now, cooperative experts Li Haochun and Li Yinbei brothers, known for their enthusiasm for social undertakings and cooperative construction movements, based on their years of practical research on rural cooperative construction, have invested their own funds to establish the China United Society. Its purpose is entirely to assist the government in completing China's cooperative construction undertaking, hoping to achieve the true mission of revitalizing the countryside. Therefore, it is completely different from other enterprises. In the vertical aspect, it is necessary to complete the three types of cooperative construction movements: consumption, production, and credit. In the horizontal aspect, it is necessary to complete the five types of vocational cooperative construction movements: education, agriculture, industry, commerce, and military affairs. Every cooperative movement starts with educational cooperation. Because the position of the education sector is the technician for manufacturing the future citizens and the mentor for the general adults in today's society, the education sector cooperates first, and other sectors rely on each other as examples. The spirit of inducing the cooperative construction movement is more important than any other sector. At present, the society has united 56 production cooperatives, 104 consumer cooperatives, and 35 credit cooperatives. It has promoted 34 production cooperatives, 68 consumer cooperatives, and 15 credit cooperatives. The number of members has reached 50,000, and the society's address covers counties along the Beijing-Shanghai line. It is hoped that the government authorities can pay attention to it, and that cooperative families, entrepreneurs, and journalists across the country can provide practical assistance. Now, in order to promote the cooperative movement in 25 counties in southern Jiangsu, including Shanghai, Jiading, Taicang, Chuansha, Nanhui, Fengxian, Jinshan, Songjiang, Qingpu, Wuxi, Changzhou, Suzhou, Kunshan, Jiangyin, Changshu, Yixing, Wujiang, Zhenjiang, Jiangning, Danyang, Jintan, Jurong, Lishui, Gaochun, and Liyang, we are particularly seeking 100 educational cooperative promoters in each county. Anyone who is employed in the education sector or is familiar with the situation in the education sector and has quick handling skills, a healthy physique, a spirit of endurance, and organizational perseverance can write a self-recommendation letter and send it directly to the Wuxi City Central Elementary School Second Branch, China United Society Office in Xixu, stating their wishes. If they are suitable, they will be invited by letter. If they are not suitable, they will not be replied. The society has also compiled a book on the six-week practical cooperative movement process, welcoming cooperative comrades to send letters to request it. The correspondence address is temporarily set at No. 25 Gaofu Lane, Baoshan Road, Shanghai Joint Manufacturing Society, Wuxi City Central Elementary School China United Society Office in Xixu.
