Ministry of Industry Revises the Implementing Rules of the Chamber of Commerce Law; Articles 14 and 5 Have Been Promulgated 167

The Ministry of Industry has revised and promulgated the articles of the Implementing Rules of the Chamber of Commerce Law, including Article 14, Article 25, Article 30, Article 34, and Article 41. The revised articles are extracted as follows: Article 14: The executive committee members and supervisory committee members of the Chamber of Commerce shall be elected by the members' congress from among the representatives by secret ballot. They shall not be apportioned by industry or self-selected by industry. The one with the most votes shall be elected. During the aforementioned elections, the county government of the county, district, and town chamber of commerce, the municipal government of the municipal chamber of commerce, the social bureau of the municipal chamber of commerce affiliated to the Executive Yuan, the industry department of the provincial chamber of commerce federation, and the Ministry of Industry of the Republic of China Chamber of Commerce Federation shall send personnel to supervise the site and implement the lottery matters stipulated in this law and these detailed rules. Article 25: The chairman and standing committee members shall report to the local competent authorities within 15 days of taking office and forward them to the Ministry of Industry for record. Article 30: In the event of any of the circumstances in Article 28 of this law, the Chamber of Commerce shall, within three days after the resolution, submit a report to the local competent authorities and forward it to the Ministry of Industry for record. Article 34: After the Chamber of Commerce is approved for record, the Ministry of Industry shall publish the seal. The seal issued by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce before the implementation of this law shall still be allowed to be used as before, except for those that conflict with this law and these detailed rules and should be exchanged. The previously issued official seals shall be returned and exchanged for seals. Article 41: The establishment of a Chamber of Commerce for Overseas Chinese shall be reported to the Ministry of Industry through the competent or nearby consulate for record. However, in places where no consulate is established and there is no nearby consulate, the Chamber of Commerce may directly report to the Ministry or request the Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee to forward it.

Qiongzhou Native Sugar Fined Case; Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests Ministry to Send Personnel for Inspection 168

Regarding the case of Qiongzhou native sugar being transported to Shanghai and detained and fined by the customs for allegedly mixing foreign sugar, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, based on the complaints of Qiongzhou sugar merchants, has sent several telegrams to the Ministry of Finance and Industry, requesting to protect the national sugar and ordering the goods to be released. The details have been recorded in previous reports. However, several months have passed and there is still no solution. The sugar merchants are increasingly worried. It is now known that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday telegraphed the Ministry of Finance and Industry again, requesting to send personnel to Shanghai to jointly inspect the samples with the customs and the receiving firms and release them quickly. The original telegram is recorded as follows: Nanjing Ministry of Finance and Industry: This month, according to a letter from Xing Juefei, representative of the Qiongya sugar merchants and the Haikou Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the native sugar transported to Shanghai by Lushou Wheel on July 24 by Haikou Jushenghao and handed over to Futianshenhang, a total of 205 packages, and the native sugar transported to Shanghai by Chongqing Wheel on August 2 by Houshenghao and handed over to Zhichengxinhang, 79 packages, the sugar was all purchased from Yazhou. When it arrived in Haikou, it was reported to the customs for inspection, confirming that it was native sugar. After paying the import tax on native goods and waiting for the wheel to be transported to Shanghai, it was also reported to the customs for inspection and paid tax in accordance with the regulations when it was exported from Haikou. The procedures were complete and the customs duties were fully paid. Unexpectedly, when the goods arrived in Shanghai, they were suddenly detained by the Jianghai Customs, accusing them of mixing foreign sugar and imposing a huge fine. If the fine was not paid, the goods would be confiscated. In this dangerous situation, the merchants could only appeal to the Central Ministry of Finance on the one hand and pay the fine with pain on the other, so as to avoid the goods being confiscated and auctioned off and it would be difficult to keep the physical evidence. It is now found that the native sugar of the two firms is still in Warehouse No. 14 of the Shanghai Taikoo Warehouse. Please allow us to forward it to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry and send personnel to Shanghai, or transfer it to the Jianghai Customs Supervision, together with your association and Zhichengxing and Futianshenhang, to send personnel to the warehouse to extract and test the sugar samples, so that the distinction between the two can be made immediately, so as to avoid the Jianghai Customs Tax Department from calling a stag a horse and making the merchants wronged, etc., to the association. According to this, it was found that from April of this year, native sugar from Qiongya was transported to Shanghai and Xianggang ports and was accused by the customs of mixing foreign sugar. The punishment and confiscation occurred almost every month. The sugar merchants there felt that they were suffering from the difficulty of appealing. The native sugar transported to Shanghai by Jusheng and Housheng was already inspected by the Qionghai Customs Tax Department when it was transferred from Yaxian, confirming that it was native sugar, paid tax in accordance with the regulations and released. The association was recorded in the document submitted to your department on October 20 by the representative with No. 358. Now, the native sugar of the two firms is permanently stored in the Shanghai Taikoo Warehouse and there is no solution. As a last resort, it is planned to request your department to send personnel to Shanghai, together with the Jianghai Customs and the receiving firms, to extract samples and verify them, so as to distinguish the true situation. It is indeed a legitimate request to exhaust all efforts and cry out loudly. It is appropriate to report the situation by telegram. Please consider and approve the request, so as to avoid delays and the suffering of the Suzhou merchants. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Yang.

Shanghai County Winter Defense Conference 170

The Shanghai County Government, as the winter season is approaching and petty thieves are prone to theft, urgently needs to organize winter defense to prevent it. Therefore, it convened a county-wide winter defense conference yesterday. The attendees were the heads of various public security bureaus, the heads of the defense regiments in each district, the chiefs of each district, and Wang Xuepeng, the chief of the first section of the county government, and Shen Zao, the chief of the public security section. The chairman was also the county magistrate Pan Zhongjia, the recorder was Ge Xiusheng, and the various cases were discussed and resolved immediately. 1. Draft a winter defense implementation plan. 2. Draft a patrol method. 3. Draft a guard method. 4. Draft interim rules for winter defense offices in each district. The above cases were all discussed, revised and passed. 5. On what date should winter defense be implemented in each district? It was decided that implementation should begin on December 1. 6. Should the winter defense period be stipulated? It was decided that it should be for three months. 7. Should tea houses, hotels, and motor ships be inspected during the winter defense period? It was decided that they should be inspected. 8. The Huijiao area bordering Songjiang County is extremely important for defense. How should we pay attention to prevention during the winter defense period? It was decided that police officers should be dispatched from the 136th branch to be stationed there permanently, and the local defense regiment should be rectified to prevent it.

Blocking the Breach Project 173

This time, the Yellow River breached a total of more than 50 large and small peaks north and south in Henan and Hebei provinces. Du Returns to Lu 175

Du Yannian, the disaster relief commissioner of the Disaster Relief Group in Shandong Province, came to Shanghai to report on the disaster situation and returned to Lu with relief tickets and relief funds the day before yesterday. The establishment of shelters and porridge factories in various disaster-stricken counties has been decided separately.

Cotton Clothes Shipped Out 176

The cotton clothes handled by the material collection and transportation section of the Disaster Relief Group were originally scheduled for 100,000 sets. Later, due to the vast disaster area and the large number of disaster victims, it was feared that it would not be enough to distribute, so 10,000 sets were specially added. The number of allocated sets was 48,000 sets in Shandong Province, 37,000 sets in Henan Province, and 25,000 sets in Hebei Province. In addition to the first two batches of 40,000 sets that were shipped out last month, the rest were all shipped out the day before yesterday to prepare for distribution to disaster victims to keep them warm.

Henan Distributes Relief Grain 177

The group's original relief method was mainly divided into emergency relief and the establishment of porridge factories and shelters. After the Henan Inspection and Release Office sent personnel to negotiate with local authorities and gentry in various disaster-stricken areas, they all agreed that setting up shelters was not easy to manage as it required a proper and large location, which would cause trouble. Therefore, it was decided to change to distributing relief grain and no longer set up factories and shelters. The situation in Hebei Province was also roughly the same.

Emergency Relief in Lanzhou 178

In addition, the Disaster Relief Group reported by the Henan Inspection and Release Office that more than 100 villages in Leiji and other villages in Lanzhou County were severely affected by the disaster, and tens of thousands of disaster victims were waiting to be fed. The office was transferred to quickly release emergency relief for relief. The relief funds have been remitted to the Lanzhou County Party Department, the County Government, the Chamber of Commerce, the Finance Committee, and the Flood Relief Association for responsible custody. In order to regulate the local economy, relief rice will be purchased locally and released in separate routes. Local publicly recommended fair gentry will be the supervisors to ensure that the disaster victims receive actual benefits.

Sino-British Communication to Realize Full Completion by the End of the Year; All Machines Have Now Arrived in Shanghai; Engineers for Trial Reporting Have Also Returned Home; The Northern Section of Underground Cable Has Been Laid 180

The Sino-British communication, after a long period of preparation by the Ministry of Communications and the British Marconi Wireless Telegraph Company, is now ready. All the machines are also shipped from the UK to Shanghai the day before yesterday. They will be transported to Zhenru by road vehicle for assembly within days. If it goes smoothly, communication can be achieved by the end of this year. As for the underground cable laid by the Ministry of Communications, a large part of it has also been completed. The details are recorded separately as follows.

All Machines Arrive in Shanghai; Regarding the machines for Sino-British communication, there are two sets. One set arrived in Shanghai long ago, and one set was shipped from the UK last month. According to reliable information yesterday, the second set of machines was also shipped to Shanghai by British ship and will be moved to Zhenru for assembly within days. There are more than 140 boxes of machines that have arrived in Shanghai this time. The machines that have arrived in Shanghai this time can be called the last batch, but there are still sporadic small parts that will also arrive in Shanghai within days.

Trial Reporting Commissioners Return Home; When the Ministry of Communications ordered the telegraph machine, in order to be cautious, it specially sent engineers Lin, Sun, Lu, and Hu to the UK to test the effectiveness of the machine. At the same time, they also took the opportunity to go to Europe and the United States to inspect the transportation facilities of various countries. The four gentlemen have now returned home.

Sino-British Communication Confirmed Date; The exact date for Sino-British communication has not yet been decided by the International Telecommunications Bureau. However, it is estimated that the installation of the machines that arrived in Shanghai this time will take one month, so trial reports may be made one month later, and formal communication may be possible on New Year's Day next year or at the end of this year.

Northern Section of Underground Cable Laid; The Ministry of Communications believes that the aerial wires from Shanghai to Liuhang are vulnerable to wind and rain, so it is now laying underground heavy cables to replace the aerial wires. The cable is divided into two sections, north and south. From Maigen Road to Zhenru is the southern section, and from Zhenru to Liuhang is the northern section. The northern section has been successfully completed, and the southern section has only been started for two or three days. There are ten pairs of aerial cables, while there are fifty pairs of underground cables. Therefore, after the success of the underground cable, it will be much more convenient than the aerial cable.

Counterfeit Currency and Coin Production Reaches Dozens of Yuan Each Night, Sold Exclusively in Jiangbei, Tongzhou, and Shanghai, the Criminals Are Separately Returned to Custody Awaiting Sentencing 188

Chinese detectives Chen Yonggui and Sun Aizhong of the Huishan Patrol House previously arrested Deng Rongting, a Shandong native, on Xinji Bang Road for selling counterfeit banknotes. They found twenty counterfeit five-yuan banknotes of the Bank of Communications and two central double-corner tickets on him. They also cracked a workshop for manufacturing counterfeit copper corner coins with molds, batteries, and other items in the stove room at No. 182 Shanqing Lane, Erjin Road, his residence. A copper coin was found in the pocket of his wife, Zhang. According to Deng's confession, the various items belonged to his fellow townsman Li Shaozhou, who lived at No. 11 Jiuru Lane, Qiujiang Road, Zhabei. The stove room was also rented by him. The detectives went to the address with the detectives of the Public Security Bureau and arrested Li. His wife, Zhou, took the opportunity to discard a counterfeit coin worth one yuan on the ground, but it was also picked up by the detectives. The patrol house sent Deng and Li and their wives and the evidence to the First Special District Court for interrogation and custody, which has been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, they were also sent to the Third Criminal Court for continued trial. Zhang Tianyin, the patrol house lawyer, stated the previous situation and presented the counterfeit banknotes, corner tickets, copper coins, manufacturing equipment, and four double-corner coins soaked in potion found on Li and Zhou. He also stated that the counterfeit banknotes and corner tickets had been verified by the two banks and were all counterfeit. The two copper coins had also been identified by a money shop. It was found that the organization could produce dozens of yuan of copper coins every night and had been doing so for more than a year, selling them exclusively in Jiangbei, Tongzhou, and Shanghai. One yuan of genuine currency could buy three or four yuan of counterfeit currency. Deng and Li, the two defendants, mutually shirked responsibility for the house and the manufacturing equipment. The second landlord of the house had left Shanghai for business and could not predict the return date. The patrol house had no way to find out who rented the house. Deng Rongting's counterfeit banknotes were said to be sold by a friend surnamed Ding, who could buy 100 yuan for 10 yuan, and he earned 1.5 yuan commission for every 100 yuan. He was a broker, and the manufacturing organization could not be found out. However, the counterfeit banknotes of the Bank of Communications were well-made and similar to the genuine ones, so many people in society must have been victimized. However, the copper coin model was probably carried and hidden by the person when it was made, and its whereabouts are unknown. The evidence against Li and Zhou, the defendants, was weak, and they were all asked to be severely punished. Deng Ting firmly stated that Li Shaozhou and a fugitive surnamed Gao came to secretly manufacture copper coins after 10:00 PM every night. He sold counterfeit coins and double corners to a friend surnamed Ding in a stove in the North Station Hanqiao area for the first time. Deng Zhang stated that Li Shaozhou and Gao did not allow them to peek when they were working. The coins copied from us were not counterfeit. Li Shaozhou stated that the house was not rented by him, and he did not help Gao to manufacture copper coins. Li Zhou stated that she had nothing to do with the case. The counterfeit coins picked up by the detectives were not thrown away by her. I ask you to identify the silver corners and potions. Judge Wu Zehan ordered Li Zhou to pay bail and be available on call, and the rest were returned to custody separately, and the sentence was scheduled to be announced.

The Fortune of a Beggar Does Not Last Long, Finding a Golden Buckle But Not Wanting to Improve, Selling Red Pills and Entering Prison 189

Zhuang Xifan, a beggar from Haimen, is thirty-seven years old. During the day, he begs for a living by picking up cigarette butts on various roads. At night, he sleeps on the streets or in alleys. Three nights ago, he suddenly had good luck. He accidentally picked up a garter on the road. He held it under the electric light and carefully examined it, and he realized that the buttons at both ends of the belt were not made of copper but of gold. He was so happy that he went crazy. The next day, he took it to a silver shop to sell it and exchanged it for seven yuan. For a time, the beggar had a small luck, and he had no idea. He thought that sitting and eating would not last long, so he planned to do a small business to make a living. However, he did not understand the tricks of peddlers and could not start. After thinking about it again and again, he came up with a way to make money easily. He envied those who sell red pills now, who can get several times the profit in one day, and becoming rich can be expected immediately. So he asked a friend who was familiar with this way to introduce him to Jiumu and obtain dozens of packs of red pills from the organization selling red pills. On the first day, he sold them to addicts in various alleys in the French Concession and made a profit of two yuan. Therefore, he still got red pills as usual on the second day and hid them to sell them in various alleys. In the morning, he earned about one yuan. Unexpectedly, on this evening (that is, on the evening of the eighth), at 11:30, he had bad luck again. He was carrying red pills and was selling them to people at the entrance of No. 6, Zhonghua Lane, Zhengjia Muqiao Street, French Concession. Just as the French patrol house detectives Hang Guangfu, Lu Songlin, Chen Tinghuai, etc. were patrolling, they saw Zhuang and stopped him for a search. Fifteen small packs of red pills were found on his body, each pack containing eighteen pills, priced at two jiao, totaling 270 pills, worth thirty jiao. He was immediately taken to the patrol house and detained. Yesterday, he was sent to the Second Special District Court. At 3:00 PM, Judge Wang Gangxu interrogated him. First, Chen Ming, the patrol house lawyer, reported the case and prosecuted him in accordance with Article 6 of the Anti-Smoking Law, and presented the red pills as evidence. Zhuang Xifan confessed to selling red pills. The red pills were purchased from an old man Qiang on Luxiangyuan Road, Jiumu, etc. The official ordered the defendant to be detained and wait for the sentence to be announced.

Apprentices Quarrel Over Copper Hooks, Resulting in Tragic Death, a File Flew into the Temple, Causing a Great Disaster 191

At Lexinglong Copper Bed Shop at No. 164 Wenyi Road, Wenzhou Road Intersection, at about 6:00 PM the night before yesterday, the partners were working when an apprentice, Zhang Aifu from Shaoxing, 13 years old, suddenly walked to another apprentice, Wang Yaotian from Anhui, 18 years old, and snatched a copper hook he was using. Wang asked for it back, but Zhang not only did not return it, but also cursed him, which led to a quarrel between the two. Later, Zhang hit Wang's right hand with a file. Wang was furious and snatched the file and threw it at Zhang, hitting his left temple, penetrating about an inch, and the brain matter came out. He immediately fainted to the ground and lost consciousness. Later, a person in the shop saw it and immediately sent him to the nearby Huilv Hospital for treatment, but he died of his injuries at about 7:00 AM the next morning. The hospital reported to the Xin Zha Patrol House, and detectives Ma Derong and Xu Huanqing went to investigate and carried Zhang's body into the Ferren Road inspection office. At the same time, Wang was arrested and taken to the patrol house. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Judge Xue took his seat and interrogated him. First, Wang Yaotang, the lawyer of the patrol house, came forward and reported the investigation process. Then he said that the cause of death of the deceased was still unknown and needed to be verified before it could be clarified. Therefore, he asked to detain the case for a week before filing a lawsuit. The court approved it. Judge Xue briefly questioned Wang Yaotian, the murderer, and the witness Jin Zhao. He then ordered the hearing to be adjourned for a week. At about 10:00 AM, the Procuratorate of the First Court appointed Prosecutor Diao Chengtang to inspect the body with the forensic medical secretary and said, "After inspection, the deceased Zhang Aifu, male, died from being stabbed in the left forehead with a file before his death." The body was handed over to his father, Zhang Amao, to sign a bond and take it back for coffin burial.

Zhou Dayuan Accuses Sheng Sixian of Abandonment, Demanding 100,000 Yuan in Alimony, the Judge Ordered the Defendant to Appear in Court for Further Interrogation 193

Zhou Dayuan, a woman from Ningbo, is twenty years old. Because of poverty in her early years, she was brought to Shanghai and fell into prostitution. Because of her beautiful appearance, she had many regular customers. In the 19th year of the Republic of China, when she was seventeen years old, she had an affair with a guest surnamed Shen. The two sides hit it off, so Shen invested money to redeem her and accepted her as a concubine, welcoming her back to live with the first wife. Because of the fear of the lioness of Hedong, unable to endure the insults, she was divorced within a year and returned to prostitution, hoping to find a satisfactory man to rely on for life. Soon after, she met Sheng Sixian, a fellow townsman. Sheng is now about forty years old and runs a foreign goods business. He has a sole proprietorship of Zhengtailong Foreign Goods Company at No. 36 Xingsheng Street in the French Concession, with considerable assets. He has a wife and children at home. Since Sheng met Dayuan, he found that Dayuan was beautiful, had a moderate figure, and was gentle in nature. After meeting, the two felt like they had met too late, so they had an affair. This spring, Dayuan became pregnant, so Sheng invested money to rent a house at No. 29 Fuming Village, Fuxu Road, and they lived together. Sheng gave her daily living expenses every month. However, although Sheng was over forty years old, he still liked women very much. In addition to his wife and concubines, he often had affairs outside. In September of this year, he had a new love and became unfaithful to Zhou Dayuan. He stopped visiting Zhou and stopped paying daily living expenses, abandoning her. Zhou Dayuan repeatedly visited him, but Sheng avoided meeting her. Dayuan was pregnant and was about to give birth, and she had no money in her hands. In desperation, she hired lawyer Lu Dingkui to file a criminal lawsuit against Sheng in the Second Special District Court, accusing him of abandonment in accordance with Article 310 of the Criminal Law, requesting that he be investigated in accordance with the law, and requesting additional civil lawsuits to recover the plaintiff's alimony and child support fees, totaling 100,000 yuan. According to the complaint, the court specially opened the Second Criminal Court to summon him for trial by Judge Xiong Huiping at 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon. The plaintiff Zhou Dayuan, who was pregnant, with her chest puffed out and her belly protruding, arrived at the court with her lawyer, and testified to the relationship with the defendant and the process of being abandoned. The defendant did not arrive, and lawyer Xu Yannian arrived on behalf of him, saying that the defendant had gone to the Hangzhou branch to settle accounts, so he did not arrive in court, and asked the court to approve a postponement of three or four days, so that the defendant could arrive in court for trial. The official then informed the defendant's lawyer that the defendant must come to court himself next time. If he avoids appearing in court again, he will issue a warrant for arrest. After the order was given, it was announced that the hearing would be adjourned to 4:00 PM on the 13th for the defendant to appear in court for further interrogation.

A Fire Broke Out in Siwen Lane Last Night, Destroying Two Buildings, Injuring Five Men and Women in Total, One Woman is Missing 194

No. 1300, No. 13 Alley, Beidong Siwen Lane, Datong Road, Xinzha Road, is jointly owned by Hua Baitao from Wuxi and Miss Xuan. The house is two buildings. Hua opened a Guangshenglong machine-rolled noodle shop in the living room for more than 30 years, and the business is very good. At about 10:30 PM last night, a fire suddenly broke out in the attic on the second floor of the shop. Suddenly, smoke filled the air, and the fire was unstoppable. In a short time, both buildings were turned into ashes. When the fire was raging, Wu Rongchu, a coal shop runner from Huzhou, a tenant on the upper floor of the living room, suddenly woke up from his dream when he heard the fire alarm. He saw that the ladder had been burned off. He and his wife, Qin, 24 years old, jumped out of the window. Wu was only burned on his face, and Qin broke his left leg. Shen, the mother of tenant Liu Sanbao, 60 years old, jumped off the terrace and injured her left waist. Her wife, Yao, 31 years old, injured her right leg. Her daughter, Bi Yun, 14 years old, fell and injured her left leg. There was also a girl named Xiudi, 10 years old, in the attic on the third floor, who was burned on both hands. The above five people were sent to Guangren Hospital for treatment by the fire department. There was also a man named Gong Hesan, 55 years old, from Wuxi, who used to be a teacher and is now unemployed and jobless, living on the third floor, who was burned on his face, hands, mouth, etc. He was sent to Renji Hospital for treatment by car. There was also a girl named Xiaodi, 16 years old, who is missing. The fire lasted for an hour and a half before it was extinguished. The houses there are densely packed and easily spread. Fortunately, the firefighters did their best to rescue them, and the neighbors were able to be saved. It is said that the adjacent Jingxin Handkerchief Factory also suffered some losses. When the reporter arrived at the fire, he saw the general victims of the fire, men, women, old and young, crying in the alley, which was very miserable.

Cotton Cloth Market Held Inaugural Meeting Yesterday 197

China National Cotton Cloth Market Co., Ltd. is a new organization that implements the boycott of Japanese yarn and cloth and plans to maintain the livelihoods of 20,000 local cloth handcraft workers. Yesterday afternoon, the company convened an inaugural meeting at its head office at No. 11 Cishuli, Guizhou Road, Nanjing Road, with more than 20 people including Wang Xiaolai attending. Hu Quewen was elected as chairman and reported the purpose of organizing the company and the preparation process. He briefly said that the organization's purpose is to focus on promoting national yarn and cotton cloth, on the one hand to assist Chinese yarn mills in developing cotton production and reduce the economic invasion of Japanese yarn, and on the other hand to do its best to promote local cloth and stabilize the lives of workers and eliminate future social concerns. With this purpose, we are combined with each other, so all facilities are slightly different from companies that are for business purposes. For example, the trainees recruited by our company, their application of felt coats, velvet shirts, shoes, socks and daily necessities, are all provided by our company, so that the trainee's family will not have any burden. In the future, within the scope of our strength, in addition to planning various methods to reduce the sales of Japanese yarn at any time, we will also pay attention to the lives and education of local cloth workers. Then, the constitution was passed and directors and supervisors were elected. As a result, Huang Renzhi, Hu Quewen, Zhang Zilian, Rong Zongjing, Wang Xianqing, Xu Caicheng, Dong Zhongzhang, Ren Jinpin, Wang Zhenfang, Du Chongyuan, and Li Dixian were elected as directors. Shi Liangcai, Du Yuesheng, and Wang Xiaolai were elected as supervisors. Then, the first board meeting was held, and Hu Quewen was elected as chairman, and Xu Caicheng, Wang Zhenfang, Zhang Zilian, and Du Chongyuan were elected as managing directors.

Landowners within these areas should promptly present their deeds for verification to obtain new land title deeds.

Hagenbeck Circus to Host Journalists 200

The German Hagenbeck Circus will host Chinese journalists from this city next Tuesday. The event will begin with a short speech by Mr. Huige Nan, an employee of the circus, on animal training, followed by a German-style banquet. The speech will reportedly detail the various methods of capturing and training lions, tigers, bears, and other wild animals, which is said to be quite interesting. Afterward, a film will be screened depicting the Hagenbeck Zoo in Stellingen, Germany, near Hamburg. The zoo, which houses a large variety of birds and animals, was created by the late Mr. Carl Hagenbeck. It took years of painstaking effort and cost millions of dollars. The zoo is now large and the animals live as if in their natural mountain habitats and caves, free from confinement and discomfort. After the meal, guests will be invited to watch a matinee performance at the circus, enjoying a half-day of entertainment.

Last Tuesday evening, Mr. Huige Nan gave a lecture at the West YMCA, detailing the methods of capturing and raising wild animals. He stated that wild and brutal methods would not work on animals, so animal trainers must first treat animals with kindness to gain their trust before they can be directed as desired. He also said that polar bears look docile, but they are the most cunning, while horses are difficult to train and require great patience. When raising wild animals, it is important to pay attention to fresh air, comfortable living conditions, and abundant food. The animals in the Hagenbeck Zoo are fed six days a week, one meal per day. On Mondays, they are not fed.

It is also reported that several days ago, Mr. Kelaibai, an employee of the circus, was hospitalized for diabetes at Baolong Hospital. His condition worsened and he eventually died. Mr. Kelaibai was born in Germany and had lived in the Far East for a long time. He joined the circus in Japan last month. He loved a Shetland pony that was very intelligent and regarded Mr. Kelaibai as a close friend. The pony followed him around the circus and never left his side. In Tokyo, the pony once escaped when the gatekeeper was not paying attention and followed Mr. Kelaibai to a coffee shop, attracting a crowd of onlookers who found it very amusing. Now that his friend has died, the pony has not eaten for two days. He is being force-fed daily, but his weight is decreasing and it is feared that he will not live much longer. This is truly amazing. Mr. Kelaibai is survived by his wife and four children. The funeral will be held at the Shanghai International Funeral Home at 2:00 PM on Friday.

Work of the China Products Improvement Society - Enthusiastic Participation from Domestic Goods Manufacturers 201

Since the China Products Improvement Society was granted a certificate by the city's Party headquarters and began its work, it has been actively progressing. In addition to submitting a filing with the Ministry of Industry in Nanjing, the Society's articles of association were recently approved by the Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters. Therefore, it is now actively recruiting members. The Society's affairs are recorded as follows: (1) Matters concerning the investigation, research, improvement, correction, and creation of domestic products; (2) Matters concerning the mediation of labor-management relations in domestic product factories; (3) Matters concerning the protection of members when they are harmed or in need; (4) Matters concerning the mediation of disputes between members or between members and non-members upon the request of a member; (5) Matters concerning requests to the government for tax reductions and exemptions; (6) Matters concerning the registration of trademarks for members or the issuance of certificates for their products to protect their circulation; (7) Matters concerning tasks commissioned or consulted by Party and government agencies; (8) Matters concerning the publicity and promotion of domestic products; (9) Matters concerning the solicitation of domestic products for exhibitions and competitions; (10) Matters concerning the organization of tours to visit domestic and foreign industrial factories and investigate the sales of their products; (11) Matters concerning the publication of regular or irregular publications and the drafting of promotional news articles, documents, illustrations, and advertisements for domestic products; (12) Matters concerning the establishment of vocational education and other public welfare undertakings. Special committees are organized: (A) (1) Raw Materials Research Committee, (2) Product Research Committee, (3) Design Committee, (4) Labor-Management Investigation Committee, (5) Finance Committee; (B) Consultants (1) Chemical Engineers, (2) Legal, (3) Mechanical Engineers, (4) Accountants, etc. According to Mr. Li of the Society, domestic goods manufacturers have been enthusiastically seeking membership recently, and a general meeting of members will be held soon. However, if members of the public and domestic goods manufacturers and businesses wish to request the Society's articles of association, please send a letter to No. 43 Zun Deli, Xiamen Road, Shanghai, and they will be mailed to you promptly.

Another Sichuan Railway Lawsuit 202

The Sichuan-Hankou Railway, which sparked the 1911 Revolution, has not been completed for over twenty years. The assets of the Sichuan Railway Company, which was organized for the project, have been nearly exhausted by embezzlement by the intermediate managers. Zhang Taijie, the president and manager, was accused of embezzling over one million yuan in public funds and was sentenced to three years in prison by the Shanghai District Court. He soon died in prison from illness. After Zhang Taijie's death, those suspected of colluding in the embezzlement, including lawyers and shareholders, have been investigated by the court. Now, Liu Yajue, a director of the Sichuan Railway, has also been accused of jointly embezzling a huge amount of money in the mortgage of the Hankou and Zhenjiang properties. The District Court has been investigating this case for years and has finally filed a public prosecution. Yesterday, Judge Qian held a court hearing. Due to the lack of witnesses, a brief interrogation was conducted, and the judge ordered a continuation of the hearing with further subpoenas.

More than a month later, the day before yesterday afternoon, Bao Yuzhen was seen by her cousin on Fuyou Road in Nanshi. The cousin took Bao's daughter to the police station. After questioning by the bureau chief, Bao's daughter confessed the details of what had happened. She said that since being lured out by Tang on September 20th, she was taken to the Tianran Hotel on Zhifu Road for two nights of adultery. Tang was afraid that the case would be exposed, so he moved her elsewhere. She was moved every few days, and her whereabouts were uncertain. On October 31st, she was sold as a wife to Jin Zhiliang for 120 yuan. Jin is a patrolman at the First Branch of the Second District. The wedding ceremony was held at the Zhixin Hotel on Wuma Road, and they have been living together in Nanshi ever since. Tang now lives at No. 199 McTaggart Road. After hearing the confession, the bureau chief immediately ordered detectives Zhu Songqing and Qu Liansheng to report the case to the Xinzha Police Station at 11:30 PM that night and request assistance. The police chief ordered detective Cai Liu and Bao detective Liu Xuecheng to go to the address and bring Tang Chengsheng and his wife, Tang Zhang, to the police station, where they were detained separately. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, stated the above situation and said that the defendant Tang Chengsheng had confessed to seducing Bao Yingdi and staying at the Tianran Hotel for two nights before moving her elsewhere, so a confession was recorded and presented to the court. However, Tang Zhang denied everything. Detective Zhu Songqing then reported the previous situation, saying that due to time constraints, he had not had time to prepare an official document and requested permission to transfer the case. Bao Wenquan also filed a complaint that his daughter had been abducted by Tang. Judge Xue Lanru briefly questioned Tang Chengsheng and his wife and ordered them to be detained separately, pending the official document from the Public Security Bureau and the transfer of the case for trial.

Carpenter Kills Mistress - Husband Only Learns the Truth After the Incident 205

A woman named Chen Lu, from Shaoxing, 28 years old, had some looks and a romantic nature. Her husband, Lu Zhiyang, worked as a cook at the Dexing Hotel on North Jiangxi Road. They lived in the kitchen of No. 9 Hongji Lane, Xinzha Road. She often went out to wander around. In June of this year, she went to a playground, where she met Lu Xingfa, a carpenter, who was also spending time there. He found her quite attractive and became very envious. He went up to talk to her, and she did not refuse, so they communicated affectionately and got along well. Since then, the two often had secret meetings, but her husband rarely knew about her affair. Recently, she became cold towards Lu, and on the morning of the 3rd of this month, at around 8:00 or 9:00 AM, Lu suddenly took a sharp axe to her house and asked her to go out with him. Unexpectedly, she refused. Lu was extremely angry at the time and raised the axe and struck her head, breaking her skull. She immediately fell to the ground unconscious, covered in blood. Seeing that he had caused a disaster, Lu immediately abandoned the axe and fled. Later, her husband was informed and returned home to send her to Baolong Hospital for treatment. He then brought her back home for treatment. The day before yesterday, she died from her injuries. After learning of this, the Xinzha Police Station immediately ordered detective Zong Weiting to investigate. He took the body to the Philen Road Mortuary and reported the case to the First Special District District Court. Yesterday and the day before yesterday, prosecutors Guo and Diao visited the mortuary successively to identify the body. According to the statement of the deceased's husband, Chen Zhiyang, 39 years old, he had gone out to work that morning, so he did not know anything about it at first. He also did not know who the murderer was beforehand. He only learned about it after the landlady came to tell him. When he returned home, he saw that his wife had been injured and Lu had fled. Yesterday morning, prosecutor Diao ordered an autopsy and found that the deceased, Chen Lu, female, had died from being struck by an axe. The body was handed over to her husband, Lu Zhiyang, to be returned for burial.

Tang Xisheng, a native of Tongzhou, opened a new tofu shop at No. 276 Zhaojia Road. It officially opened a few days ago. They called for the police Liu Kaizhi from the Second Branch of the First District to arrest them. The case involves gathering a crowd to extort money. These kinds of unemployed vagrants specialize in extortion and are harmful to society. They must be severely punished to deter them. This issue is a special issue on children's books nationwide. In addition to collecting and introducing more than 5,000 kinds of children's books published by the publishing industry nationwide, it also includes more than 20 articles on forums on children's books, children's library science, and literature, written by famous scholars. In addition, there are more than 1,000 indexes of the latest new books and social science works nationwide. The breadth of the collection and the richness of the materials are unprecedented. It is a necessary reference for libraries, community education centers, and primary schools nationwide. The next issue will be a special issue on traditional Chinese medicine books. It has been compiled for many years and includes all medical books from ancient times to modern times. It is estimated that there are about 30,000 to 40,000 books listed, and there are dozens of articles by experts in traditional Chinese medicine. It is truly an unprecedented creation in the field of traditional Chinese medicine. The two journals are priced at 40 cents each, and the special issue on traditional Chinese medicine is priced at 80 cents. Subscribers for the whole year (1.50 yuan) will not be charged extra. The subscription locations are the Zhejiang Circulation Library on Gulou, Hangzhou, and the Modern and Author Bookstore in this city.

▲ Modern 500 Family Circle Poetry Collection Mr. Yu Xiangcao, a Confucian scholar from Nanhui, once wrote two circle poems that were divinely inspired and were hailed as masterpieces. Mr. Zhu Taimang, also from Nanhui, took them and wrote poems in response. He collected poems from poetry circles in various provinces for ten years and compiled them into a collection entitled Modern 500 Family Circle Poetry Collection. It contains more than 1,700 poems, with an appendix of Circle Poetry Talks. There are more than 30 authors, each writing poems in which the circle in the title must be present with a meaning different from the others, with an emphasis on pleasant or suggestive imagery and humor. The resulting collection is indeed an original development among poetry collections. Now it is being printed and sold by Guangyi Bookstore on Qipan Street at a special price of 65 cents per copy, including postage. A directory of the names of the 500 families is printed. Please enclose a one-cent stamp for postage when requesting a copy.

▲ A Brief History of Traditional Chinese Medicine Mr. Zhang Zanchen, a physician at No. 77 Xiangkang Lane, Baker Road, recently wrote the book A Brief History of Traditional Chinese Medicine. The book discusses the medical affairs of the Zhou, Qin, Han, Tang, Song, Jin, Yuan, Ming, and Qing dynasties. It also discusses materia medica, gynecology, pediatrics, massage, surgery, ophthalmology, beriberi, cholera, measles, bubonic plague, consumption, guidance techniques, recuperation methods, incantation, medical history, medical cases, tongue diagnosis, medical journals, and the integration of Chinese and Western medicine. The references are extensive and the analysis is detailed and clear. It is a great work in the medical field. The special price is only 48 cents.

Second Day of the Zhejiang Provincial Secondary School Principals' Meeting ▲ Resumption of the Second General Assembly 218

(Hangzhou Correspondence) The situation on the first day of the Zhejiang Provincial Secondary School Principals' Meeting has been recorded in this newspaper. On the morning of the 9th, group meetings were held, and teaching and organizational groups separately reviewed [items]. From 1:00 PM to 4:00 PM, the second general assembly was resumed, attended by 26 people, with Chen Youlei as chairman. The meeting proceeded as usual, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) Promote educational research among secondary school teachers and staff; (2) Stipulate measures to supervise and assess the evening self-study of boarding students; (3) Regarding how to guide junior high school students in their further studies, guidance should be based on educational policies and address existing malpractices, so that students can be assigned to appropriate schools according to their aptitudes, nature, and environment to benefit education; (4) Secondary school principals with special circumstances may request a reduction in concurrent positions; (5) It is proposed to reduce the teaching hours of full-time teachers in secondary schools to improve efficiency; (6) Outstanding students from elementary school graduation exams in each county who are admitted to the junior high department of provincial secondary schools within the school district should be exempt from written exams; (7) It is proposed that the monthly salaries of full-time teachers and staff in secondary schools below 60 yuan this year be paid at 97.5% of the actual value, as in the case of affiliated elementary schools; (8) Provincial education funds should be designated from provincial tax items and a management method should be established to ensure security; (9) How should the excessive arrears of funds for each school be relieved to benefit education; (10) Regarding the Ministry's order to stop collecting registration fees from the 13th academic year onwards, how should each school seek relief and remedy; (11) It was resolved that the review report of the moral education group would be reserved for discussion at the third general assembly; (12) Conduct an education fund security campaign, and issue a "Letter to the Elders of Zhejiang" in the name of the Provincial Secondary School Principals' Conference. Ye Suzhong, Tang Shifang, and one other school principal were designated to draft it; (13) It was resolved to extend the original three-day meeting by one day. After 4:00 PM, the administrative group and the finance group resumed group meetings. In the evening, Yu Jingsheng, manager of the Hangzhou branch of the Commercial Press, hosted a banquet for the principals and educational staff at Jufengwei. Shen Jieshun, head of the Hangzhou branch of the China Bookstore, distributed various books published by the bookstore yesterday afternoon. (Sent on the 9th)

Ministry of Education Official Letter 221

To Whom It May Concern: The outline of teaching subjects and class hours for various subjects in vocational schools has been determined and announced by the Ministry. The curriculum outlines for vocational subjects and vocational practice teaching materials, as well as the equipment standards for each subject, in various vocational schools need to be compiled separately to facilitate teaching. Please follow the prescribed methods to compile the curriculum outlines for vocational subjects and vocational practice teaching materials for vocational schools, and the equipment standards for each subject, and send them directly to the Ministry within one month for review. Your cooperation will be greatly appreciated. Attached are three sheets of the list of schools entrusted to compile, four copies of the Compilation of Vocational Education Laws and Regulations, three copies of the Matters to be Noted for Compiling the Curriculum Outlines for Vocational Subjects and Vocational Practice Teaching Materials for Vocational Schools, and the Equipment Standards for Each Subject, and two copies of the Compilation Forms.

Matters to Note 223

Matters to note when compiling curriculum outlines and equipment standards for vocational schools: (1) Before compiling, the Vocational School Law and Regulations and the Outline of Teaching Subjects and Class Hours of Various Subjects in Vocational Schools must be carefully consulted; (2) Vocational subjects refer to the theoretical subjects of knowledge and lectures in each subject; vocational practice refers to the skill practice subjects of each subject; equipment for each subject refers to all the minimum equipment that should be available for practice in each subject; (3) The teaching materials and teaching procedures of vocational subjects and vocational practice should progress from simple to complex, from manual work to mechanical work, and from simple machines to complex machines. Special attention should be paid to the teaching materials of the times; (4) For each unit of practice, attention should be paid to all aspects of the unit, such as purpose, raw materials, tools, methods, management, estimation, assessment, and the time required for learning; (5) The equipment of each subject should be listed separately, and the quantity and the number of people who can be accommodated for practice should be noted.

Standard Format 224

Drafting Form for Equipment Standards of Various Subjects of Vocational Schools, "School Compiling" ○○ Category ○ Grade ○○ Subject Equipment Standards for Vocational Schools "Category", Machinery, Instruments, or Specimen Models, Tools and Implements, Medicines, Other Equipment, Category of Practice Place, Area of Practice Place, "Name", "Quantity", "Price", "Purpose", "Number of Trainees", "Remarks", Explanation, (1) The equipment of each subject is different. This form is an example. The compiler can add or subtract according to the actual situation. (2) The number of trainees in each subject is based on the standard that all practice places can accommodate 70 to 80 people.

Obstacles to Centralizing Education Fees in Jiangyin 227

Jiangyin's education fees have become increasingly strained in recent years, and the situation has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Ying Zixiu and Xu Zhengji, from the academic circles living abroad, advocated that at a time when the county's educational finances are in dire straits, with more than eight months of education fees owed throughout the county, in order to centralize education, they specifically telegraphed the Department of Education and the county government to incorporate all assets of various academic societies into the education funds to avoid waste. However, Jiang, the head of the Southeast Township School, instigated his cronies to oppose it. It is reported that fellow villagers from Shanghai, Beijing, Suzhou, and Zhenjiang will send letters to urge the Education Bureau to take over, to uphold the law and maintain education.

Ministry of Finance Orders the Consolidated Tax Bureau to Stop Issuing Special Education Funds; Hebei Province's Education Funds Are Fundamentally Shaken 228

There is also talk of reducing 360,000 yuan for the expenses of national universities in Beijing and Tianjin

Education Fee Protection Committee Recommends Li Zheng to Go to Beijing to Visit Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi

(Special dispatch from Beiping) The education funds of Hebei Province are specifically funded by the consolidated tobacco tax. Recently, the Hebei Financial Special Commissioner's Office was reorganized into the Hebei-Chahar-Suiyuan Consolidated Tax Bureau. The bureau did not issue education funds, so the education funds of Hebei Province were fundamentally shaken. Wei Yuanguang, a representative of the Hebei Provincial School Federation, came to Beijing on the 6th. That evening, Tingjin also promoted Yang Shaozhong, Qi Guoliang, and Li Banghan as representatives. The three representatives arrived in Beijing today (the 7th). When the reporter visited Yang at his residence, he said the following:

Yang Shaozhong Speaks 229

The total education funds for Hebei Province are more than 3 million yuan per year, of which 1.2 million yuan is a special education fund. This special fund was stipulated by Zhang Zongchang in the 15th year of the Republic of China to be allocated from the consolidated tobacco tax, with a monthly allocation of 100,000 yuan. The expenses of each school rely on this for support. The remaining amount is allocated by the Hebei Provincial Government ordering the Finance Department to find ways to allocate it. The education special fund is allocated by the Hebei Financial Special Commissioner's Office. Now the Special Commissioner's Office has been abolished by order of the Ministry of Finance and reorganized into the Hebei-Chahar-Suiyuan Consolidated Tax Bureau. The bureau has been ordered by the Ministry to temporarily suspend the issuance of the education special fund, and all kinds of negotiated funds are to be reported to the Ministry of Finance for approval. The funds will be allocated after approval. In fact, the education special fund has long been designated to be allocated from the consolidated tobacco tax and is not a negotiated fund. It is a special fund in nature and is completely different from a negotiated fund. If the special fund is suspended, the education funds will be shaken, and the education of the entire province will be bankrupt. The goals of the representatives in coming to Beijing this time are two: (1) The nature of the education special fund is different from other negotiated funds and the authorities should be requested to allocate it monthly; (2) The education special fund is eight, nine, ten, and three months in arrears and requests that it be made up. First, a petition will be filed in Beijing. If there is no satisfactory result, personnel will be sent to Beijing to visit Minister Kong to deal with it in person.

(Special dispatch from Beiping) The expenses of national universities in Beijing and Tianjin are 360,000 yuan and there are rumors of a reduction, which has caused great panic among teachers and staff. The Beijing-Tianjin Higher Education Expenses Management Committee has, in addition to telegraphing the Ministries of Education and Finance to urge the remittance of the October education expenses, also recommended Li Zheng as a representative to go to Beijing for negotiations. Li left by train today (the 7th). Before leaving Beiping, Li made the following remarks to reporters:

Li Zheng Speaks 230

I am going to Beijing this time for three tasks: (1) To negotiate the expenses of higher education in Beijing and Tianjin. There are rumors that the central government will reduce the education expenses of colleges and universities in Beijing and Tianjin. It remains to be investigated after arriving in Beijing whether this is true. The Management Committee entrusted me to negotiate in Beijing. As I am also a member of the Management Committee, I should of course fulfill my obligations. After arriving in Beijing, I will separately visit Minister of Finance Kong (Xiangxi), Minister Wang (Shijie), and Mr. Li Shizeng to request the authorities to allocate education fees on time every month. The higher education expenses in Beijing and Tianjin are 260,000 yuan per month, which is allocated from the Russian Boxer Indemnity Fund. The Ministry of Finance instructs the National Treasury Department to allocate it to the Beijing-Tianjin Higher Education Expenses Management Committee every month, obtain the receipt of the Management Committee, enter it into the income assets, and report it to the Minister of Finance. This method was approved by Minister Song (Ziwen). Now that Minister Kong has taken office, the procedures for allocating the expenses of colleges and universities in the future may not be changed, but there must also be a negotiation and the October education expenses must be urged; (2) To report to the Ministry of Education on the school affairs and progress plan of the Normal University and to negotiate on the new curriculum standards; (3) To handle the higher examination assistant examination matters. Originally scheduled to go to Beijing on the 10th, I started earlier because I received a telegram from the Examination Yuan.

Two Telegrams Urging Payment 231

Telegram to the Ministry of Finance: Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance, Nanjing, I am very happy to see you take charge of the finances. The Beijing-Tianjin Higher Education Expenses of 260,000 yuan were previously submitted to the committee for remittance to Ping before the 25th of each month, which has been approved. Now the October expenses have not yet been remitted, and each college and university is finding it very difficult to cope. Please order the remittance of the funds as soon as possible for transfer and distribution. Respectfully, the Beijing-Tianjin Higher Education Expenses Management Committee, fish, telegram to the Ministry of Education, Minister Wang of the Ministry of Education, Nanjing, the October Higher Education Expenses for Beijing and Tianjin of 260,000 yuan has not yet been remitted, and it is very difficult for each college and university to cope. Please inform the Ministry of Finance and remit it as soon as possible for transfer and distribution. Respectfully, the Beijing-Tianjin Higher Education Expenses Management Committee, fish.

River-Zhejiang Private Secondary School Football and Basketball Tournament Scheduled to Be Held in Suzhou 235

This year's River-Zhejiang Private Secondary School Football and Basketball Tournament, according to previous guidance meetings by the various schools, has been decided to be held on December 13th, 14th, 15th, 16th, and 18th (Gregorian calendar) at Soochow University in Suzhou. Citywide Mobilization of Primary School Students: Municipal Primary School Games Open Yesterday; Numerous Track and Field Events, Four Types of Running Races for Boys and Girls; Diverse and Ingenious Group Performances 237

The fifth annual Joint Primary School Games, organized by the Municipal Education Bureau, opened yesterday at 9:00 AM at the Municipal First Public Sports Field. Mayor Wu did not attend due to a cold, and the opening speech was delivered by Chairman Pan Gongzhan. Yesterday, only the preliminary 100-meter races for boys and girls in each group, as well as the preliminary rounds of the softball throwing event and the standing long jump finals for girls in each group, were completed. Details are recorded as follows:

▲ Students from Municipal First Kindergarten Performing Planting Flowers (Photo by Qichang)

Opening Ceremony 238

▲ A Glimpse of the Venue: Yesterday, the weather was clear, and the primary school students were all in high spirits. The entrance to the Public Sports Field on Dalin Road was bustling with people and vehicles. Outside the short bamboo fence surrounding the venue, students from various schools stood guard, with brightly colored flags fluttering in the wind. The stage was set up in the north of the venue, with a white cloth banner hanging above that read, "The Fifth Annual Joint Primary School Games of Shanghai Municipality." A pair of couplets hung beside it: "Gather all Shanghai primary school students to test their physical education" and "Promote the Chinese nation and enhance martial prowess." Several pots of chrysanthemums were placed on the stage, and a portrait of Sun Yat-sen with the Party and national flags crossed in the center. The Public Security Bureau and the Shanghai Poor Children's Home military band arrived to play music. The East Asia Boy Scouts and the Southern District Security Corps maintained order.

▲ Chairman's Address: The opening ceremony was held at 9:00 AM. After raising the flag and playing music, Mr. Pan Gongzhan, the chairman, delivered a speech, stating briefly that today is the opening of the fifth annual primary school games in the city. The mayor was unable to attend due to a cold and sent Mr. Gongzhan as his representative. Our country has reached a critical moment of life and death. If we do not revive our country soon, it will perish. To escape the danger of extinction and achieve the goal of revival, our youth must take responsibility. The purpose of the primary school games is to train the physique of every primary school student so that they can shoulder the responsibility of saving the country in the future. He hoped that everyone would work hard and persevere.

Speeches from All Sectors: Subsequently, Mr. Lin Meiyan, the representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, delivered a speech, stating briefly that the first thing we should do in sports is to be hygienic and not harm the body for the sake of winning championships. Secondly, we must be collective and not focus solely on the individual. Thirdly, we must popularize sports so that they can deeply penetrate the people. Then, Honorary Instructor Huang Zaoxiong delivered a speech with many words of encouragement.

▲ Report on Meeting Affairs: Finally, Secretary-General Shao Rugan reported on the affairs of the meeting, stating briefly that there are 32 track and field events in this year's games, including 20 for boys and 12 for girls. There are 108 participating school units, 1,591 track and field athletes, and 53 schools participating in group exercises, with a total of 183 sections. After the report, the group exercises began, and the sports activities commenced.

Group Performances 239

Many schools participated in the group exercises this time. On the first day yesterday, there were 19 sections in the morning and 46 sections in the afternoon. Due to time constraints, performances from five or six schools were held simultaneously in the afternoon. For a time, the venue was filled with the sounds of music, voices, commands, and the clashing of dumbbells, which was very lively. The orderly steps and graceful movements aroused the excitement of the entire audience.

Overwhelming: Huasaishi Defeats Youyou ▲ Result: 8 to 4 245

Huasaishi, newly arrived in Shanghai, drew 1-1 with Jinan in the Shigaota Cup. At the time, observers examined their approach and probed their strength, concluding that they were by no means mediocre. In yesterday's friendly match against Youyou, they showed their true colors, defeating Youyou 8-4. It was clear that their skills were excellent, and they were indeed a first-class team.

Overview of the Two Teams 246

Huasaishi is full of talent. The five forwards are agile and quick-footed. Center Moleen is the leader of the group. The defense is very strong, and the interior is well-organized with few gaps. Youyou's inside defenders, Lu Zhiming and Cheng Guoyin, lack strength and experience. The defense is not good, but the forwards work hard. In the first half, they succumbed to the iron cavalry, ending 1-3. In the second half, they made great strides, tying the score at 4-4. Unexpectedly, their momentum collapsed, and they lost four goals, ending in an 8-4 defeat.

Course of the Match 247

Referee Chen Jixiang blew the whistle, and the fierce battle began. Before long, Huasaishi's center Moleen broke through the line, and Youyou was caught off guard and conceded a goal. After ten minutes of intense fighting, right winger Shepote benefited from the center's assistance and scored again. Youyou launched a counterattack but missed several opportunities. Suddenly, Moleen again broke through the line, making it 3-0. Youyou was furious, and the entire army advanced. Center Hu Youcheng broke through the enemy's goal, making it 3-1 at halftime, with Huasaishi in the lead. At the start of the second half, Youyou veteran Zhu joined the team, boosting the morale of the entire army. They attacked more than they defended and had hopes of recovering. Unexpectedly, in the midst of their strong momentum, they were hit by the enemy's Aguerre, making it 1-4. The former elite spirit was still there, and they were very active in the enemy's formation. Li Shuoyou tried a shot, and it unexpectedly hit the mark, making it 2-4. From then on, their demeanor changed completely, and Youyou's momentum rose. Within ten minutes, Hu You and Chen Jiaqiu each scored a goal, tying the score at 4-4. The good times did not last, and bad luck struck again. Moleen, in the midst of thousands of troops, was as if in no man's land, scoring one, two, three, and four goals, making it an 8-4 victory.

▲ Youyou Team
